(Nanjing) Ba Wanjun, a counselor previously dispatched by the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Council, traveled to Tibet via detour in May to meet with the Dalai Lama and convey the intentions of the Central Committee. He also went to Nepal to meet with the King of Nepal. After the resolution of the dispute between Tibet and Nepal, Ba left Tibet and returned to the country via India. He is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 19th. The gifts from Tibet and Nepal to our country are as many as dozens of boxes and the Council has dispatched personnel to Shanghai to take care of them. (Seventeenth Special Dispatch)

Xuzhou Holds a Meeting to Clear Up Vehicles

(Xuzhou) The meeting to clear up vehicles on the Jinpu, Jiaoji, Longhai, and Pinghan Railways was held at the Garden Hotel at noon on the 17th. Qian Zongze presided over the meeting, and Railway Department members Li Yue, Tang Hua, and Xu Chuanyin attended to supervise. More than ten representatives from the four railways attended. The Transportation Headquarters proposed a vehicle clearance plan, and the representatives also had proposals. The resolutions are yet to be announced. Qian told reporters at the scene that with the end of military transportation, the vehicles urgently needed to be cleared up. However, the relationship between the four railways was complicated, and discussions would take time. This meeting may require an extended period, but the overall goal is to obtain a proper clearance method. (Seventeenth Special Dispatch)

Transportation Between Hunan and Hubei Resumes

(Hankou) The damaged tracks, telegraph, and telephone lines on the Hunan-Hubei Railway have been repaired. The express train from Changsha to Wuchang arrived at Wuchang Station on the 17th. At the same time, the express train to Changsha also departed. The Railway Bureau is planning to restore all passenger and freight trains. (Seventeenth Special Dispatch)

Three Lines of Northeastern Army Placed Under the Control of Yu Xuezhong

(Peiping) Yu is scheduled to return to Peiping on the 18th and then transfer to the Peiping-Hankou Line. Currently, Zhang has ordered all the Northeastern Army troops on the Peiping-Suiyuan, Peiping-Hankou, and Zhengtai Lines to be under Yu's command and control, unifying authority. Currently, the Northeastern Army on the Peiping-Suiyuan Line has no intention of advancing west of Chaigoubu. The Jingxing area on the Zhengtai Line will also have to wait for the Jin Army to withdraw before advancing. This is because it is firmly believed that the Jin-Sui conflict will be resolved peacefully in the near future and there is no need for urgency. (Seventeenth Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Jin Danqing, Commander of the Northeastern Artillery, has recently expanded the artillery by three regiments. Liu Fusheng is the commander of the first regiment, Zhang Sigong is the commander of the second regiment, and Zhu Lihan is the commander of the third regiment. They will be formed by the end of this month. The first and second regiments will be stationed on the Jilin-Heilongjiang border, and the third regiment will be stationed in Peiping and Tianjin. (Seventeenth Special Dispatch)

(Peiping) After Shi Yousan returned to Shunde, he immediately complied with the order to downsize his troops. The artillery headquarters was abolished, and Lin Jiaxun was reassigned as a councilor. The original designations of the two armies and the First and Second Training Divisions were all abolished. They were reduced to two divisions, with Shen Kemi and Wen He serving as division commanders. Soldiers who retained their weapons remained, while those without weapons were dismissed. Tianjin Municipal Water Price Issue

(Tianjin) The municipal government, because the British-owned water company pays 360 taels annually, which is the amount for 20 years, recently sent people to investigate its business, but was refused. On the 17th, it convened a meeting of the social affairs, public safety, land, and finance bureaus, and decided to order a reduction in water prices, otherwise, increase the amount paid. If this is not accepted, it will be taken back. Fortunately, the company has no contractual restrictions. (17th)

International Important Telegrams

Hamaguchi Escapes Danger

Discharge of Gases Twice, Life No Longer in Danger

Assassin Charged with Attempted Murder, News Articles Banned from Newspaper Publication, Imminent Convocation of Parliament, Parties Busy Reorganizing Their Ranks, Government and Parties at a Loss

▲Tokyo Telegraph, 17th (Dentsu): There was much doubt regarding changes in Prime Minister Hamaguchi's injury. At 1:15 AM last night, he continued to fart twice, releasing a large amount of gas from his abdomen. Those nearby were overjoyed and celebrated. Secretaries Nakajima and Toda immediately notified the parliamentary group and party offices of the farting news. Worried party members cheered "Hurray!" Secretary Toda even composed a poem praising the Prime Minister's fart and opened champagne to celebrate. This was the first time there was wild jubilation since the Prime Minister entered the hospital.

▲Tokyo Telegraph, 17th (Dentsu): After the Prime Minister farted, there is now hope for his life. His condition continued to be good today, and the Prime Minister himself is confident that he is no longer in danger. His spirits have been greatly lifted.

▲Tokyo Telegraph, 17th (Nichiren): The assassin who shot Prime Minister Hamaguchi, Ryou Yuuki, was indicted on charges of attempted murder on the evening of the 16th. At 11:05 AM on the 17th, he was escorted from the Metropolitan Police Department to the prosecutor's office. After being detained and questioned by preliminary trial judge Akiyama, he was placed in the Ichigaya Prison in the afternoon of the same day. Due to the criminal investigation, news articles about Ryou Yuuki are banned from publication from this day forward. However, at 2:00 PM on the 17th, the ban was lifted only for the release of the assassin's name, age, address, and background by the Metropolitan Police Department as follows: Ryou Yuuki, the assassin who shot Prime Minister Hamaguchi, is 23 years old, originally from Tomisato Village, Higashisonogi District, Nagasaki Prefecture, and currently resides at the Aikoku-sha office in Nagatacho, Kojimachi Ward, Tokyo. According to the assassin's testimony, he was born in Dalazi, Jilin Province, China. After graduating from elementary school in Korea at the age of 15, he left home and lived with his mother (who had divorced his father) in Ito's home in Fukuoka Prefecture. He then worked as a sailor between Moji, Yokohama, and Kobe until the age of 19. Afterwards, he wandered around the Manchurian region for about a year. At the age of 20, he secretly sailed from Dalian to Singapore. He came to Tokyo the following year in October and lived in various places. He has been a member of the Aikoku-sha since mid-July.

▲Tokyo Telegraph, 17th (Dentsu): With the opening of Parliament less than 40 days away, each political party is busy planning how to deal with Parliament. The Minseito Party, in particular, is facing an extremely erroneous situation in terms of its parliamentary lineup due to Prime Minister Hamaguchi's misfortune. They are currently at a loss as to who should lead the parliamentary battle. If Prime Minister Hamaguchi has not fully recovered by then, whether Interim Prime Minister Shidehara Kijuro will act as proxy to deal with it, or whether someone else will be replaced, the parliamentary lineup will change accordingly. Therefore, this is the primary question. The party leaders are quite worried about the lineup as they are at a loss as long as the Prime Minister Hamaguchi's condition is not definitely determined. They are currently remaining silent. On the other hand, the Seiyukai, faced with an absolute majority, is preparing for this three-month regular session of Parliament for the first time. They plan to have the party's elite stand at the forefront. Kishi Keisuke, the former Minister of Home Affairs, is being strongly advocated for the position of the leader of the parliamentary group. They will also select capable speakers such as Tobu, Uchida, Oguchi, Uehara, and Horikiri to raise issues such as the economic recession, the budget, supplementary plans, national defense, and other urgent issues such as measures to address rice prices and unemployment, and launch a fierce attack from the start to pressure the government.

International Important Telegrams II

Indian Round Table Conference

Work Has Already Begun

Nehru Sentenced to Imprisonment and Fined, Public Outrage, Major Demonstrations Held

▲London Telegraph, 17th (Reuters): The Indian Round Table Conference began work today. The affairs of St. James's Palace have been divided into two sections: one dedicated to procedural matters, and the other to discussing the constitution of India, whether it should be based on a central system or a federal system. Whether the meeting should be open or closed has not yet been decided.

▲London Telegraph, 16th (Reuters): British Indian representatives held another informal meeting at St. James's Palace yesterday. After the general assembly on the 17th, they also plan to hold another informal meeting on the 18th. The Maharaja of Baroda gave a speech at the East India Association's reception, saying that the representatives attending the Round Table Conference come from all parts of India. Although the provinces they represent, their beliefs, customs, races, and languages are not entirely the same, they are united in their determination to reach an agreement to obtain the best interests for India. This is the guarantee of India's ultimate success. The safety and greatness of the British Empire depend on listening to the Indian people to freely develop what India needs according to their talents. India should be one of the self-governing members of the British Empire. This is India's inherent right. The British should promise to proceed forward together with the Indian people who know their responsibilities with mutual trust and cooperation.

▲Bombay Telegraph, 17th (Reuters): The President of the All-India Congress Committee, Nehru, was arrested again on October 19th. Because Nehru had just been released from prison and gave a speech at the assembly in North Allahabad, the authorities accused him of inciting the public to destroy the salt laws and refuse to pay taxes. The case opened on October 24th. Nehru was unwilling to respond. On the 29th, the court sentenced him to two years of imprisonment, with hard labor, and a fine. In various parts of India, there is great dissatisfaction with this judgment. There are now frequent demonstrations to protest. Yesterday, Bombay police used batons to disperse demonstrators in two clashes, injuring several people and arresting many people. There was a large parade in New Delhi, which was also dispersed by the police. 218 people were arrested. In the Surat region, clashes between the public and the police injured 100 people.

Spanish Labor Unrest Shows Significant Revolutionary Tinge

Rumors Spread Along the French-Spanish Border, Authorities Confident of Containing the Seeds of Disorder

▲Madrid Telegraph, 16th (Kokumin): Following the general strike in the Spanish capital, it is now effectively surrounded by military police, and the revolutionary tinge of the labor unrest is becoming increasingly pronounced. Currently, traffic is blocked, taverns and public entertainment venues are all closed, and security forces patrol the streets wearing steel helmets. However, the workers are still able to maintain order by complying with the union's orders. The government declares that if there is any disturbance in the capital, martial law will be declared immediately.

▲Paris Telegraph, 16th (Kokumin): Direct communications from the Spanish capital are quite hindered due to censorship, and therefore rumors are spreading along the French-Spanish border. According to a report from Hendaye today, riots broke out in the Spanish capital this afternoon, especially in the suburbs. There are also reports of unrest in Barcelona.

▲Madrid Telegraph, 16th (Reuters): A strike was declared here on Saturday and Sunday, but not by everyone, nor was there any rioting. All stores, including cafes and taverns, are closed, but the vegetable market remains open, so there is no shortage of food. Crowds gathered outside bakeries to purchase bread. Only two newspapers are published and delivered by army trucks. The central railway is still running, and the city's cleaners are working as usual. Military police patrol worker-dense areas to prevent accidents. The Spanish Prime Minister stated today that the authorities have sufficient strength to deal with any possible disturbance. The government has implemented various methods to maintain a sufficient supply of food for the capital's citizens, and said that this strike is completely unreasonable.

▲Madrid Telegraph, 17th (Reuters): The Labor Party leader issued a declaration advising strikers to resume work no later than 5:00 PM tonight. A total of 250 people were arrested yesterday. The capital is quiet today. Soldiers are baking bread ceaselessly throughout the day.

Polish General Election Held

Pilsudski Faction Securely Occupies Majority, Minor Disturbances in Southwestern Provinces

▲Warsaw Telegraph, 17th (Kokumin): Although reports of vote counts from several districts of the Polish preliminary election have not yet arrived, the current known numbers are as follows: the Pilsudski Defiance Faction has a total of 246 seats, a much greater increase than the previous 125 seats. The right-wing opposition National Democratic Party had 37 seats in the previous session, and now has 53 seats. The leftist opposition had 175 seats in the previous session, and now only occupies 70 seats. The Marxists had 34 seats in the previous session, and now have only 25 seats. Germans have 4 seats, Jews have 10 seats, Christian Democrats have 15 seats, and the Communist Party previously occupied 7 seats, and now has only 5 seats. The total number of seats in parliament is 444. Counting the above results, only 16 seats remain, and it is unknown to whom they will belong.

▲Warsaw Telegraph, 16th (Kokumin): Today, general elections were held throughout Poland. The preliminary reports are as expected, and the Pilsudski faction can securely occupy a majority. However, whether they can obtain two-thirds of the 444 seats to create a dictatorial government through a major constitutional amendment is still difficult to say. The final results of the election will likely be revealed tomorrow night. According to news received from various places tonight, the country is generally peaceful. Only a few minor conflicts occurred in eastern Galicia, and there were also minor disturbances in Polish Upper Silesia.

▲Tokyo Telegraph, 17th (Nichiren): The Ministry of Colonial Affairs received a telegram stating that at 10:10 AM on the 16th, a small team of aborigines suddenly sneaked into the forest about 300 meters in front of the Harada Unit of the Maihanbao Detachment and opened fire on our team. Minister Wu Gave a Radio Broadcast Speech

Said that China Is Molting from the Medieval Period into a New Era, Continuous Unrest Is an Inevitable Stage of World Revolution

▲Washington Telegraph, 16th (Associated Press): Chinese Minister Dr. Wu Chao-chu stated during a radio broadcast at 2:30 PM today that China's unrest is actually the first result of nearly five simultaneous revolutions. If the same situation occurred in Western countries, such a situation would occur one after another instead of all at once, but the results of the disturbance would still be similar. China is currently molting from the medieval period and entering a new era of national life. Therefore, the nation's intellectual, economic, social, and nationalistic aspects are all undergoing great changes. Whenever there are such major changes, associated repercussions are inevitable. This can be seen in various countries. The American Revolution was not achieved until after the Civil War was settled. The French Republic took a chaotic 80 years to establish itself. It is like a baby in swaddling clothes, who is often plagued by measles, whooping cough, and other symptoms that come and go. China's situation is the same, except that all the symptoms occur at the same time and without any order.

Important Domestic News

Central Government and National Government Commemoration Week

▲The Central Party Headquarters held the 86th weekly memorial service for the late Premier Sun Yat-sen at 8:00 AM on the 17th in the Grand Auditorium. All members of the Central Supervisory Committee and Central Executive Committee who attended the Fourth Plenary Session, as well as Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang, and all officials from various departments and councils of the Central Government, participated, totaling about 600 to 700 people. After the ceremony led by Chairman Yu Youren, Li Yuying reported, stating briefly that the comrades of the Central Government had already reported on party affairs, politics, military affairs, and other major issues, which should be clear to everyone, and there was no need to repeat them. Today, he wanted to give a brief report on the chronological order of the National Revolution and the North-South unification. The revolution originated in the southwest of China and gradually extended to the southeast. The period of close relationship with the northeast was also very long. In the twelfth year of the Republic [1923], he met Comrade Zhang Hanqing [Zhang Xueliang]. He immediately recognized him as a person of outstanding talent and profound sympathy for the revolution. When the Premier was alive, he wrote a personal letter to Comrade Zhang, inviting him to work together to save the country. Comrade Zhang still keeps this letter as a memento. Later, as the revolutionary forces grew stronger and the political situation in the north changed, Comrade Zhang, due to environmental factors, was unable to make a clear statement immediately, but his attitude of sincere cooperation with the National Revolution was always tacitly understood. This is an indelible historical fact. China is vast, and in the past, there was an emphasis on the distinction between North and South, but in reality, it was only a difference in local customs and the speed of development of water conservancy and transportation. The national spirit has always been the same. Recently, Comrade Zhang has especially refuted entrenched views, eliminated prejudices, and promoted the true unification of North and South. The generals in the Northeast have all understood Comrade Zhang’s painstaking efforts to maintain peace and unification and relieve the suffering of compatriots. They followed the Premier’s teaching of "peaceful struggle to save China" and unanimously supported the Central Government, so that China, which had not been peacefully unified for twenty years or was only formally peacefully unified, could achieve permanent peace and unification, in order to calmly engage in construction and vigorously become a newly emerging country. This is the greatest good fortune for the future of the Republic of China. Therefore, the chronological order of time and space is quite remarkable. He previously visited the arsenal in Shenyang, and its scale was grand, truly the best in the country. Recently, the policy has been to prepare to convert most of the manufacturing of military equipment into production manufacturing. From this point of view, his mentality of maintaining peace can also be believed. Next, Zhang Xueliang reported briefly that he had served in the military for a long time and deeply knew the pain and suffering of the military and civilians during wartime, which was even more severe than what everyone had heard or read in writing. He recalled that once when passing through Mamuji, he saw disaster victims after the war lying all over near the train station, barely breathing, with no color on their faces. He asked why they were here and why they were displaced and not returning home. The disaster victims cried and told him that it was not that they did not want to return, but that they had no home to return to. Their wives and children were scattered, and their fields and houses were in ruins. Even if they returned, they could not make a living. At that time, he felt very sad and realized that these tragedies were all caused by the military. Everyone has a family, parents, wives, and children. Mistaken by the concept of force at one time, the people are plunged into eternal doom. What a great crime. Therefore, his outlook on life has also changed. During wartime, both sides consider each other as enemies and only know how to kill and destroy without any scruples. But those who are killed are all the brave sons of China. If this mentality is used to resist foreign aggression, how glorious it would be. Instead, compatriots kill each other, and people of the same race oppress each other, disregarding the country and the people, and willingly become criminals who destroy peace. How can they justify themselves in conscience? The source of the communist disaster was also caused by civil war. Therefore, he vowed to devote his utmost sincerity to support the Central Government and complete peaceful unification. If the goal can be achieved, he would not hesitate to grind his head to the top. Furthermore, any criticism must be based on a thorough understanding of the truth of the matter, as well as the past and the future, before it has value. It is like climbing a mountain, you must follow a certain path and climb step by step to the summit, so that you can see everything above, below, left, right, before, and behind. If you climb with artificial feet from a dangerous and narrow path, you will inevitably fall in the middle. He believes that once something is done, you should not be afraid, if you are afraid, you should not do it. You should take everything openly, etc. After the report, the meeting adjourned at 9:00 AM.

▲The National Government held the weekly memorial service for the late Premier Sun Yat-sen at 10:00 AM on the same day. He Yaozu, Ma Fuxiang, Jiang Menglin, Liu Ruiheng, Zhang Nanxian, Zhu Lixue, Chen Yi, Chen Shaokuan, Zheng Hongnian, Mu Xiangyue, Wang Jiazhen, Li Jinlun, Chen Yu, Zhang Wohua, Zhu Jingnong, Zhou Yawei, Wu Siyu, Zhang Xiqian, and more than 200 officials from the National Government’s civil service and military affairs departments attended. After the ceremony led by Chairman He Yaozu, Secretary Qian Changzhao gave the following political report: "The most important thing in the country last week was of course the birthday of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen and the opening of the Fourth Plenary Session. The birthday of the late Premier was on the 12th of this month, and the opening of the Fourth Plenary Session was also on the 12th of this month. The birthday of the late Premier was the day when a new life of China sprouted, and the opening of the Fourth Plenary Session was the day when a new life of China grew. (The resolutions of the Fourth Plenary Session will be reported in full after the closing ceremony.) Now that Feng and Yan have been eliminated and unification has been achieved, we can follow the late Premier’s deathbed instructions to 'peacefully struggle to save China.' The so-called peace refers not only to domestic affairs, but also to international affairs. On the one hand, we must save the country from no more wars, and on the other hand, we should take on the responsibility of maintaining permanent peace in the international community. With peace, we can actively struggle. There are two most far-reaching ways to struggle, one is spiritual, and the other is material. Spiritual struggle is to reform social psychology, and material struggle is to develop natural resources. To reform social psychology, we must first establish a moral standard, and everyone must start with themselves. If you have made mistakes, you should reflect and awaken. Then, look at the evil and corrupt forces in society and try to influence them and eliminate them. As long as the majority of people work hard on this, spiritual civilization will not be difficult to maintain. Developing natural resources is also equally important. The people's livelihoods are not affluent because natural resources have not been fully developed. But to develop natural resources, we must first lay a scientific foundation. Compared with other countries in the world, the foundation of science in our country is already far behind. Furthermore, even though science in other countries has progressed, there are countless things in the universe that should be known but are not known, and that can be used but are not used. Our country, as a country with backward science, should continue to research and explore. As long as the majority of people work hard on this, material problems will not be difficult to solve. The above-mentioned spiritual and material struggles can easily achieve results in a peaceful environment. Therefore, struggle must also take the path of peace. If we can peacefully struggle, then China can live in the 20th century without fear. Regarding foreign affairs, I have already talked about the issue of self-determination for the peoples of the Far East twice. The non-violent resistance of India has had a great impact. The British hope to resolve everything through the Round Table Conference. The Round Table Conference opened on the 12th of this month with 86 representatives, including 57 from British India, 16 from the Indian princely states, and 13 from the British Parliament. Before the official opening, there were several informal discussions. The British are very optimistic about the future of the conference, but we see that no one from the Gandhi faction has joined, and on the opening day, the Indian Catholics went on strike again to express their grief. So, even if the Round Table Conference has good results, whether the Indian issue can be resolved from then on is still unknown. The number of Taiwanese aborigines is small, and the equipment is not complete. Openly resisting powerful Japan is like an ant trying to stop a cart. The result is of course failure. But whether their lives can be improved in the future after this struggle and sacrifice depends on Japan's actions."

In the summer of this year, the 56th Division was transferred to the province, and Gao's department took over the defense of Quanzhou. The people's团 of Jinjiang Nan'an counties once联合驱高, and then the provincial government调防 Gao's department to Huian. The Huian people also suffered after Gao驻惠. At the beginning of this month, Gao Weiguo sent his ministry to Lin Jianwu Gao Yang鑼营 to 开驻 Dongyuan of Huishou. On the 7th, he first sent people to Dongyuan to find the address of the驻兵. The people of Dongyuan Township refused because Gao's department's discipline was too bad, and the two sides had a conflict. At 8:00 a.m. on the 8th, Gao sent Lin Gao's two ministries of 500-600 people to attack Dongyuan in three ways. The fierce battle was very fierce, and Gao's troops returned to Changban Township. On the morning of the 9th, Gao's troops attacked Daicang again, and the people's teams guarded it to the death. Gao's troops could not win, so they washed away the surrounding five townships of Changban and went to Huian People's League Head康伯沧 sent a team of 50 people, and 辎川 People's League 20 people, to help one after another, 合 Dongyuan Changban's various district people's leagues, and the乡民 who joined the hoe, no less than 1,000 people. Local Correspondence

Jinshan

The school principal was stripped of his clothes and robbed. Ding Tiejun, the principal of the fourth central elementary school in Qian'an, lived in Lvhetan and habitually returned home in the evening. On the afternoon of the 12th of this month, when he was returning home from school, he suddenly encountered more than 30 bandits, holding six rifles, two box guns, iron rulers and wooden sticks. They grabbed Tiejun, stripped off his clothes, top hat, leather shoes, and robbed him of forty-eight yuan in cash and banknotes, as well as his briefcase. His glasses were also smashed. They tied his hands tightly with hemp rope and dragged him to Chen Wenjun's house at the east end of Qian'an (only one mile away from Qian'an) to rob. First, they attacked the front and back doors, but they were unbreakable, so they entered through the stove window. Tiejun was tied to the bed, and then all of Chen's valuables were robbed. The doors and windows were also smashed. Fortunately, the family had already escaped, so there was no harm. Only one person was seriously injured by the bandits, and it is unknown whether there is any danger. After the robbery, the bandits released Tiejun. Tiejun was quite cold, so he put on the broken quilt left behind and returned.

Songjiang

The new director of the Construction Bureau takes over. Xu Wei, the director of the Construction Bureau of this county, was ordered by the province to leave his post, and Sun Shengzeng, the director of the Construction Bureau of Nanhui, succeeded him. The newly appointed Director Sun came to Songjiang yesterday to take office. After Director Xu handed over the bureau affairs, he immediately left the bureau with his family.

Strictly implement the National Calendar holiday for elementary schools. Since the National Government ordered the implementation of the National Calendar, all sectors should abide by it consistently. The Education Bureau believes that schools are the object of public attention, and holidays should be absolutely observed in accordance with the Education Department's instructions. Fearing that the elementary schools in the countryside, accustomed to old habits, might be insincere, it was decided at yesterday's bureau meeting that, in addition to ordering all education committees to comply, special personnel should be sent to inspect the situation in various places. The National Calendar holiday is three weeks, and the lunar calendar should not be given a holiday.

Suzhou

The detective team arrested suspected bandits who robbed a boat. Sun Renfu's night boat between Suzhou and Guangfu was intercepted and robbed by bandits at about 3:00 a.m. on the 8th of this month when it was sailing to Dongkuatang. More than 400 yuan in cash was robbed. Afterwards, the victim reported to the Public Security Bureau for arrest. After the bandits obtained the property, due to uneven distribution of the loot, three bandits, Yang Jigen, Liu Xingxing, and Zhang Jiaxiang, met Zhou Hongjiang, the captain of the detective team of the Public Security Bureau, on the road outside Chanmen on the evening of the 15th. They went forward to surrender and reported that the bandits were hiding in a village house near Xintang Bridge behind Huqiu. After receiving the report, Captain Zhou lured them to open room 19 in the Zhonghua Hotel, and separately reported to the Public Security Bureau and summoned many detectives from the entire team. At about 1:00 a.m. that night, they drove to Huqiu with Wang Du, a patrol officer from the free car team. They arrived at Xintang Bridge at 4:00 a.m. the next morning and searched according to the address. They arrested suspected criminals Zhang Fengpei, Zhu Ruilin, Li Shisheng, Qin Jilong, Li Yusheng, Su Genda, Zhao Genfa, Zhu Jinshan, Li Fangming, Li Shuru, Liu Desheng, Liu Qinshi, Zhang Liushi, Li Pengshi, together with Yang Jigen, a total of 17 men and women, as well as stolen embroidered clothes and other items. They were handed over to the team at 6:00 p.m. on the 16th, and will be handed over to the bureau for investigation after interrogation.

Customs Treasury bonds were transferred to the Provincial Treasury again. Wuxian was ordered to raise 250,000 Customs Treasury bonds, which were offset by the conversion of grain transport. The county magistrate and the financial officer successively raised 200,110 yuan from the banking industry. In addition to the 180,000 yuan that had been transferred to the province earlier, yesterday (17th) it was transferred to the Jiangsu Bank for transfer to the Provincial Treasury, and the Finance Department was also informed that there was still a surplus and there was no way to prepare, so please end it.

The trial court opens the case of patricide. In the Qijiaqiao area of Zhabei, Shanghai, Sun Laowu, a native of Nantong, was killed by his adopted son Sun Liansheng, along with Ji Shuangquan, Qiu Shuntao, and Qiu Lansheng. The Shanghai District Court sentenced Sun Liansheng and Ji Shuangquan to death, Qiu Shuntao to life imprisonment, and Qiu Lansheng to 15 years in prison. The defendants refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the High Court. Yesterday (17th), the Criminal Third Court of the High Court opened a trial court and changed the date to summon witnesses for trial.

Changshu

The winter defense district chief builds three conferences. The county government of this county opened a winter defense meeting yesterday morning. The district chiefs of each district and the captains of the water and land public security teams attended. County Magistrate Tan presided over the meeting. The decided items are summarized as follows. Regarding joint defense matters, it was decided to divide the county's 15 districts into six major joint defense districts. Each district will have one director and several deputy directors, and temporary military telephones will be set up to receive news and facilitate defense. Unemployed guests and vagrants will be ordered by the public security sub-bureaus and outposts to strictly ban their comings and goings, and residents will be prohibited from retaining them. The meeting ended at 12:00 noon. In the afternoon, district chiefs' meetings and fundraising closure meetings for the construction of prisons were held. At the district chiefs' meeting, the decided items included, as proposed by the first district chief, whether the activity funds for the district branch should be deducted from the district financial management office. The result was that the county government would submit a request to the Civil Affairs Department for verification and approval. The fundraising for the construction of the prison has now ended, and the results are quite good, reaching more than 6,000 yuan. In the future, for construction matters, a Changshu County Prison Construction Committee will be organized, and nine committee members will be appointed: Qu Junyi, Chen Qiwei, Xu Jingxi, Qu Liangshi, Hao Bingzhang, Wu Zhongying, Xu Juntan, Wu Xinheng, and County Magistrate Tan. The base will use one and a half mu of land from Daonan Company in accordance with the Land Acquisition Law of the National Government, and will be submitted to the county government meeting for deliberation.

The peanut boat in Fushantang was robbed. A Jiangbei guest Shi, who specializes in selling peanuts, came to Changshu the day before yesterday to sell peanuts. After selling the goods, he calculated that he had more than 600 yuan in cash. For the convenience of hiding, he went to the Transportation Bank to exchange banknotes, and then set sail from Changshu to return to his native Jiangbei. Unexpectedly, Shi was侦知 by bandits when he sold the goods and when the boat arrived at Xieqiao, it was already dark and he could not travel. Shi and others rested there. At 4:00 a.m. the next morning, the sky was still not bright. Due to the tide, Shi and others drove the boat to start. Unexpectedly, after passing Chenjiaqiao, the place was 冷僻. Three bandits shouted to stop the boat on the shore, and they had to wait for inspection. Shi and others saw that they were inspectors and did not suspect anything else, so they leaned on the shore. The three bandits jumped on the boat and searched the entire boat, each with a box gun. As a result, more than 600 yuan in goods was robbed and escaped ashore.

There are doubts about the giant extortion of associates in Huahang. Chen Mingkui, an associate of the Yu Kang Cotton Shop in Hejia City, came to the city and withdrew a huge amount of 17,500 yuan from the Bank of China. The case of being robbed on the way was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that after Chen Ziyoucheng withdrew the money, he put the banknotes in a rattan basket and took the Zhitang ship back to his hometown. After paying 100 yuan at the tax card, he walked back to Hejia City. When he arrived at Zhudian Bridge, he met four bandits. Two bandits robbed Chen's rattan basket first, and two bandits pushed Chen from the bridge to the river. He was rescued by someone, but the bandits had gone far and could not be traced. Chen Na淋漓 went to the He City Xingzhong and reported to the manager, and then转报 the armed forces to pursue the bandits. However, according to the villagers from Zhitang, the headquarters of the Yu Kang Flower Shop is located in Wuxi. Every autumn, they must come to Changshu Wujiang to collect cotton. Chen Mingkui is indeed an old friend of the company with a good reputation. There are many suspicions about this giant extortion: (1) Since the robbers extorted his money, why did they push him into the river again? (2) The ship can reach a certain place three miles away from He City, but Chen Deng'an on the more distant Zhitang, although there is a tax card relationship, but you can also go to Xinghou and then pay again. (3) The area is heavily defended, and cases of robbery are rare. All of the above are speculations from the villagers. Now, due to the importance of this case, the defense agency has sent various teams to the countryside to investigate.

Wuxi

The Public Security Bureau divides the Wuxi area into five police districts. In the past, there were 17 cities and towns in Wuxi, and later they were changed to 17 autonomous regions. The entire county's public security sub-bureaus have the largest number in the first district, with six sub-bureaus. The remaining 16 cities and towns have only ten sub-bureaus. The establishment has not been widespread, so the districts that have not established sub-bureaus have not been covered by each other, and there is a feeling of neglect in terms of security jurisdiction. Xu Jigui, director of the Public Security Bureau, was keenly aware of this and specifically brought this matter up at the sixth bureau meeting. It was decided to divide the county's public security sub-bureaus into five districts, with one sub-bureau in one district as the principle. Depending on where the sub-bureau is located, the district will be the directly managed area. The adjacent districts that have not established sub-bureaus will be temporarily assigned to the nearby sub-bureau for co-management. After the sub-bureau is established in the district in the future, it will be returned. Yesterday, the descriptive text of the division of police districts was submitted to the county government for approval and record.

Expel the inferior monk from Xilin Temple. There is a Xilin Temple outside Ximen Bridge, welcome to Dragon Bridge. The abbot of the temple, Monk Canxia, is originally from Jiangbei. He is lewd in nature, does not abide by Qing regulations, and organizes a lotus society in the temple to seduce young men and women, promote superstition, collect money and confuse the public. Recently, he has been blinded by greed and has occupied the old five-hole bridge bridge alley near the place, colluding with his fellow villagers to build grass sheds, obstruct pedestrians, and hinder traffic. The people in the area, You Houqing, Wen Jinxian, Zhang Tong, etc., believe that the monk's behavior is illegal, so yesterday they jointly submitted a letter to the county government with 44 merchants such as Hongtai in the area, requesting that the adulterous monk Canxia of the temple be expelled from the country as soon as possible and another abbot be recruited.

Jiangyin

Jiangyin's autumn harvest is fully levied according to the amount. Most of the counties in Jiangnan have had bumper harvests this year. Jiangyin did not report any disasters, and the autumn harvest should be fully levied according to the amount. Yesterday, Director Shen of the Finance Bureau reported the detailed numbers of the silver and rice actually levied this year to the Finance Department, totaling 985,592 mu, 2 li, and 8 hao of real flat fields, and the amount of upper and lower busy silver was converted into 213,245 yuan, 6 jiao, and 6 li, 5 hao. The amount of Cao rice was converted into 380,269 yuan, 5 jiao, and 4 li, 6 hao.

Zhenjiang

Strictly arrest the wanted criminals in the Zhaoyang Cao malpractice case. The Jiangsu Provincial Government, in the case of Zhou Bisen and Wang Lingping reporting the loss of Cao grain in the previous year's Liyang bandit chaos, Zhang Quan, Zheng Chengyuan, the former county magistrate, and various party and government agencies in the county all colluded to commit fraud and share the spoils. Previously, personnel were dispatched to conduct a thorough investigation and successively transferred 11 people, including Zheng Chengyuan, the county magistrate, and Pan Bin, the director of the Finance Bureau, to the province for interrogation. All of them were suspected of serious crimes and have been transferred to the Zhenjiang District Court for legal interrogation. There are still important criminals in the case, including Zhang Quan, the former county magistrate of Liyang, Cheng Linshen, the former director of land tax, and Zou Hanliang, the former section chief of the finance bureau, who have not yet been arrested. Therefore, yesterday, the Civil Affairs Department was specifically instructed to transfer the order to its subordinates to strictly arrest them all and bring them to justice for investigation.

Yangzhou

Conspiring to Seduce and Abscond with Funds: Outside the city's customs gate, there was a farmer named Chen Tingkui, who had a daughter named Xiao Bianzi. She had been betrothed to a son of the Wang family. Some time ago, Chen went to the town on business. A shop assistant named Yin Zhengliu, working in a clothing store next door, took advantage of Chen's absence. He conspired with a friend named Xiong to seduce Chen's daughter and abscond with funds. Unexpectedly, they were spotted halfway by a neighbor named Jin Yusheng. After Chen returned home, Jin immediately informed him of the situation. Thereupon, Chen immediately apprehended Yin Zhengliu and handed him over to the local former Baojia head for custody. Subsequently, Yin requested Sheng Yuhuai to intercede, promising to hand over the person the next day. However, he failed to fulfill his promise. Chen, having no resolution, then sued Yin and others at the local Public Security First Branch for conspiring to seduce and abscond with funds. It is said that after the branch received the complaint, it considered the case related to judicial matters and inconvenient to handle, and instructed him to directly file a lawsuit with the court.

Aircraft to Arrive in Yangzhou Soon: The airfield established outside the East Gate of this city, according to orders, is now ready. Yesterday (the 15th), eighty barrels of airplane fuel were transported from the provincial capital. It is said that the military department will soon dispatch two airplanes to Yangzhou to assist in suppressing bandits.

Lvsi Town Telegraphs Bandit Alarm: The Huai River Transport Commissioner's Office received a telegram from Lvsi Town, stating that bandits there, united with bandits from neighboring towns, burned and looted nearby villages and towns, taking everything. They also forcibly demanded a large sum of money from the Lvsi Town Magistrate. When he refused, they kidnapped the Magistrate and demanded a ransom. Fortunately, the Magistrate heard the news and fled, avoiding disaster. However, the area has been devastated. They requested that the telegram be forwarded to the Salt Affairs Bureau, requesting the dispatch of a large force to suppress the bandits. Yesterday (the 15th), the telegram was forwarded to the Salt Affairs Bureau, and the Huainan Anti-Smuggling Bureau was ordered to suppress the bandits.

Conflict Between Anti-Smuggling and the Defense Corps: The Second Battalion of the Huainan Anti-Smuggling Infantry, under the jurisdiction of the Public Security Bureau in the Haimen area, while dispatching teams for patrols and anti-smuggling, repeatedly encountered misunderstandings with the local village defense corps, resulting in conflicts. Now, Battalion Commander Wang of the battalion came to Yangzhou on the 13th. Yesterday morning (the 14th), he went to visit the Director of the Anti-Smuggling Bureau, presenting the previous reasons and requesting instructions on how to handle the situation.

Rugao

Firefight Between Sea Bandits: It is said that the Haigang sea bandits have long been divided into two factions, the Southern faction led by Pan Kaiwu and others, and the Northern faction led by Shen Guanxi and others, who have been harassing the coastal areas. Last autumn, Shen was recruited by Ma Yuren and led his troops to participate in the harassment of Yancheng and Funing. After the failure, he again led his troops south to the ports in the area. Unexpectedly, Shayutingzi had been seized by the Southern faction, Pan Kaiwu, and others. Shen, feeling that he had been deprived of his territory, was unwilling to give up. He led his men to attack Pan's bandits, sinking as many as nine of Pan's ships with artillery fire. Pan led his ships to retreat from the port. The day before yesterday morning, Pan suddenly commanded a large number of followers, leading more than 30 ships, and attacked Shen's troops again. Shen's bandits could not resist and gave up the port again. The port's terrain is advantageous and has long been occupied by them. The current firefight is due to this reason. It is said that the fighting between the two sides was quite fierce and the losses were great.

Bride's Homecoming, Husband Killed: Miao Wenlin, the grandson of Miao Shitiao, a farmer in Dongjiao Xiexing Township, Libao, was 21 years old. He was the heir to two branches of the family. He had been newly married for just 29 days, and was planning to accompany his bride to her parents' home for the homecoming visit the next day. He came to the town to take a bath at 4 PM today (the 11th). While passing in front of the Public Security Bureau, he suddenly encountered five soldiers from an unknown team, armed with rifles and Mauser pistols, escorting two rickshaws, each carrying someone resembling a farmer. They ordered him to pull the rickshaws. After traveling less than a mile, Miao Wenlin ran away in an attempt to escape. The soldiers followed and fired a shot from a Mauser pistol, hitting Miao Wenlin in the head. He fell to the ground, his brains splattered out, a tragic sight. The deceased's family rushed to the scene upon hearing the news, wailing and crying. The Public Security Bureau and the District Defense Corps of this town heard the news and pursued them, but the perpetrators had already escaped without a trace.

The district chiefs of the entire county went to the province together, along with the victims. With the court date of the 18th approaching, a telegraph request was made to extend the trial by two weeks.

County Magistrate Inspects Jingxin Middle School: On the morning of the 11th, County Magistrate Shen personally went to Jingxin Middle School to inspect it, in accordance with the regulations on awarding those who donate funds to promote education promulgated by the ministry, and to investigate the situation and expenses. The school is located on the beach outside the East Gate, at the former Gu Family Pavilion. The school building is very spacious, with the cost of purchasing the land and construction being no less than 50,000 yuan. The opening expenses alone have already spent about 4,000 yuan, all donated solely by Mr. Zhu Jingxin. After the county magistrate inspected all parts of the school on that day, he believed that it was in line with the regulations promulgated by the ministry and would submit a request for reward.

Huzhou

Bandits Spreading in the Western Countryside: The banditry in the Changxing area of the western countryside of Huzhou has been rampant recently, surpassing other places. Kidnappings and robberies are heard every day. In Yangjiaqiao, about nine miles from the Dadongmen of Changxing, there was a farmer named Yang Adong, who was engaged in farming and had considerable property. At about 8 PM on the afternoon of the 12th of this month, suddenly a dozen or so bandits came, each holding a wooden-cased gun, suddenly arriving at his house, breaking down the door and entering, overturning boxes and cabinets, searching at will, looting all the silver dollars and valuables, and kidnapping Adong's son, leaving a letter demanding a large sum of money. When the bandits left, they fired shots to show their power and went in the direction of Lijiaxiang.

Also, in Panjia Village, outside the West Gate of Changxing, there was a resident named Zangpin Xuan, who had a well-to-do family. Late at night on the 10th, suddenly about 20 bandits speaking in mixed accents came, each holding pistols, wooden sticks, and daggers, and broke in the door. At that time, Pinxuan and his family were all asleep and could not escape. The bandits did not rob anything, but kidnapped Pinxuan's son and someone from a certain village, leaving a letter demanding 65,000 yuan, to be paid at a certain place, etc.

Hefei

Resolution of Dispute Between Chamber of Commerce and Stamp Bureau: The County Chamber of Commerce learned that Fang Bocheng, an inspector of the Stamp Tax Bureau, changed the amount of a single bill issued to Ai Hongxing's small goods store at the city gate from one yuan and one jiao to eleven yuan and one jiao, and also removed a new one-fen stamp and replaced it with an old one-fen stamp, deceiving the bureau chief and punishing Ai Hongxing for both revealing and missing stamps for ten yuan. The Chamber of Commerce felt this was unreasonable and seriously negotiated with the bureau, proposing three conditions: remove Fang, apologize, and guarantee that this would not happen again. The bureau has accepted all three conditions, removing Fang and issuing a formal apology.

Zhejiang Education Department Investigates County Education Funds

▲ Formulating Investigation Forms... Issuing to Various Counties for Verification and Filling

The Zhejiang Education Department, in order to investigate the education fund assets of various counties and the district education funds, recently formulated three types of forms and distributed them to various county governments to fill out in detail according to the forms and report them for record within one month of receiving the documents. The content of the forms is as follows: A, Education Fund Investigation Form, (1) Amount of Funds in the Province, (2) Annual Interest Rate, (3) Amount of Interest, (4) Use of Interest and Remaining Amount, (5) Depository Institutions and Evidence Numbers, (6) Current Capital and Interest, (7) Explanation. Attached form explanation, (1) In the (item) row of this form, the name of the fund, such as the elementary school fund (remaining profits from vagrant bonds), academy deposits, Binxing funds (public quota fees), Dengying Association fees, and the names of all other deposits should be filled in separately. If there are too many items, another page can be attached. Public debt securities should be filled in as an example for deposits, and the "Amount of Capital" should indicate how many bonds and the face value. (2) "Annual Interest Rate" should fill in the annual interest rate, such as monthly calculations, should be converted to annual, "Amount of Interest" refers to the total annual interest, "Use of Interest" refers to the designated use, for example, the interest of the elementary school fund is used as a reward for excellent teachers, or other county education fees, academy deposits, used as the regular expenses of the county elementary school, etc. "Remaining Amount" refers to the remaining amount after the allocated use (Depository Institutions and Evidence Numbers), the location of the deposit such as the bank, money shop, pawnshop or other business name and the deposit book number and the last two characters of the bond should be filled in, (3) All numbers should be filled in using Arabic numerals, not other types of fonts, to unify the format, (4) This form should be filled in duplicate and submitted at the same time, (5) If there is any situation of the fund deposit book being pledged externally, it should be filled in detail in the (Explanation), (6) Other matters that are not listed in the various cells of this form should also be listed in detail. B, Education Asset Investigation Form, Items, (1) Houses and Land, (2) Fields, (3) Land, (4) Mountains, The items are divided into one, asset quantity, two, usage status, three, rent and interest rate, four, income amount, five, rent and interest usage, six, evidence number, seven, explanation. Attached form explanation, 1. Asset quantity, the column should fill in the asset, such as the number of houses, divided into buildings, flat houses, etc., and the number of acres, points, cent, mills, etc. of the land. 2. The (Usage Status) column should fill in the original case for what purpose, (the property of a certain education institution), now it is for own use, (school buildings, halls, clubhouses, etc.) or leased, (rented to open a certain type of business), etc. 7. Other items should be filled in by referring to the (Education Fund Investigation Form). 4. This form should be filled in triplicate and submitted at the same time. C. District Education Expenditure Investigation Form. 1. Income in the 18th year, 2. Comparison of increase or decrease in the 17th year, 3. Estimated increase or decrease in the 19th year, 4. Original case and current use, 5. Collection and rectification methods, 6. Explanation. Attached form filling explanation, 1. The item column of this form should list the names of all district education funds of a certain character in the county by category, and the tuition fees collected should also be listed as one item, without any omissions. If the increase or decrease in the 17th year is greater than, then fill in ten geometry yuan, if the decrease, then fill in one geometry yuan, the following four or five people, (estimated...) column imitates this, (Rectification Methods) are formulated by each county, 3. All numbers should be filled in using Arabic numerals, not other types of fonts to unify the format, 4. This form should be filled in duplicate and submitted to the department.

▲ Deciding the Date of the Plenary Session ▲ And Holding an Exhibition of Teaching Materials and Teaching Aids

The Jiangsu Provincial Experimental Elementary School Federation held an executive committee meeting on the 14th of this month in Zhenjiang, at the Zhenjiang Middle School Experimental Elementary School. Local News

Declaration of the Seventh District Party Department on the China Public School Incident

▲ Students Suddenly Expel Ding Kouyin

(National News Agency) The Seventh District Party Department declared on the China Public School incident, saying, At the time when the military is pacifying and the central government is planning reconstruction, all sectors of the people should strive for the development of their careers to save China, which is in danger. However, in recent days, student movements have repeatedly occurred in schools in Beijing and Shanghai, which does not seem to be the hope for the future of construction. Among the student movements, the China Public School is the most prominent. The reason for this is that those responsible have failed to patiently guide the young students to the correct path of the Three Principles of the People and have provoked and instigated them afterward, leading to repeated disputes and delays. Since Hu Shi took over as president of the China Public School, erroneous theories and heresies have emerged one after another, defaming the Premier and sparing no effort. After criticism from our party comrades, he left the school. He was succeeded by Ma Junwu, who, in order to consolidate his position, did not hesitate to protect reactionary elements, colluding with them and using the hot-blooded youth to control the student union and rape the will of all the students. After being pointed out by social figures, he resigned and left the school. The board of directors, out of love for the China Public School, could not bear to sit idly by, so they urged Mr. Yu Youren to maintain it. Anyone with a little conscience should unanimously support and sincerely welcome it. Who knew that Hu Shi and others would cause trouble, instigate the movement, and their vicious intentions are evident here. The comrades in this district, not wanting to sit idly by, specially spoke out righteously. On the one hand, they hope that Wang Gong will continue to take responsibility, and on the other hand, they warn Hu Shi not to be a scourge of society. They hope that the youth will work hard at their studies at this time of construction and talent need to complete the Premier's will. This is the declaration.

Record of the Shanghai County Education Bureau's Bureau Affairs Meeting

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held a memorial week yesterday morning and then held the 175th Bureau Affairs Meeting. Attendees included Director Shi, Supervisor Zhu, Zheng Guozhai, Sun Tingfang, Lin Weiwen, Niu Zhiyi, Yang Huiming, Yan Chongguang, Yao Juechen, Cai Xingsan, Yao Xingshu, Wu Renda, Fan Xingsan, Chairman Shi, and Recorder Pan Xingsan. The ceremony was conducted as usual, and the report items were omitted. Next, the discussion: (1) Reviewing the proposed administrative organization plan of various elementary schools by the division, it was resolved (1) to pass it and order the schools to study it first (2) the implementation period was set to begin in the second semester of the 19th year. (2) Reviewing the school equipment survey form, it was resolved to ask Niu Zhiyi and Yang Huiming to revise it and then submit it to the next meeting for discussion. (3) Holding the school arts and sports competition for this semester, it was resolved (A) the intermediate grade Chinese, common arithmetic, and measurement test will be held on December 7th, with fourth-grade students participating. (B) The senior grade Chinese speech will be held on December 14th, with sixth-grade students participating. The detailed methods above will be stipulated by the School Education Division. (4) The date of the establishment meeting and the first regular meeting of this administrative committee, it was resolved, will be held at 3 PM on December 3rd. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Shanghai Middle School Experimental Elementary School's Centennial Savings Fund Filed

The Shanghai Middle School Experimental Elementary School of Jiangsu Province, located on Shangwen Road in this city, in view of the fact that the education expenses in Jiangsu Province have always been stretched, each school feels the need for reality on the one hand and the difficulty of allocation on the other when preparing the budget, always feeling stretched. Therefore, there is a centennial savings fund, taking 100 yuan of national currency from the regular expenses of the 18th year, and storing it in the Shanghai Commercial Savings Bank on August 1st of the 19th year, according to the bank's wholesale deposit and withdrawal, compound interest of one point calculated every ten years, ten turns is a period of one hundred years, and the amount will reach more than 1,729,200 yuan. However, since the savings fund is long-term, it is necessary to carefully consider the management method. Therefore, the savings fund regulations were formulated and submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department and the Jiangsu Provincial Government for record. It is said that the school received an instruction from the Education Department yesterday, stating that the method of establishing a centennial savings fund is well-intentioned, and the various management methods are also detailed, and permission is granted to forward it to the Provincial Government for review and record. From then on, the foundation of the school will be more solid, and future development will be unlimited.

Schedule of the 10th World Games

▲ Men's 50,000-meter Race Walk Added - Women's Javelin and Low Hurdles Added

(Los Angeles News) The 10th World Games will be held in Los Angeles, USA, in July of the 21st year of the Republic of China. The games will last for half a month and will include track and field, all-around, swimming, equestrian, shooting, boxing, fencing, rowing, and various ball games (only tennis is not included, as there is the Davis Cup every year). The track and field program of the Games has been decided by the organizing committee and officially announced, notifying all countries participating in the contract. The Japan Association of Athletics Federations received this official notice on the 12th of this month. The content is slightly changed compared to the previous session. A men's 50,000-meter race walk has been added, the women's 800-meter has been eliminated, and the javelin and low hurdles have been added. The schedule of the track and field all-around program of the Games is as follows:

▲ First Day (July 1st)

400-meter Intermediate Hurdles Preliminary, High Jump Final, Shot Put Final, 100-meter Preliminary, 800-meter Preliminary, 100-meter Semi-Final, Intermediate Hurdles Semi-Final, 10,000-meter Final, Women's Javelin Final

▲ Second Day (July 2nd)

Hammer Throw Final, 100-meter Final, Intermediate Hurdles Final, Women's 100-meter Preliminary, 800-meter Semi-Final, Women's 100-meter Semi-Final, 3,000-meter Steeplechase

▲ Third Day (July 3rd)

High Hurdles Preliminary, Long Jump Final, Women's Discus Final, 200-meter Preliminary, 800-meter Final, Women's 100-meter Final, High Hurdles Semi-Final, 5,000-meter Preliminary

▲ Fourth Day (July 4th)

5,000-meter Race Walk, 200-meter Semi-Final, Pole Vault Final, Discus Final, Women's 80-meter Low Hurdles Preliminary, High Hurdles Final, 200-meter Final, 1,500-meter Preliminary

▲ Fifth Day (July 5th)

400-meter Preliminary, Javelin Final, Triple Jump Final, Women's Low Hurdles Semi-Final, 1,500-meter Final, Women's Low Hurdles Final

▲ Sixth Day (July 6th)

Decathlon 100-meter, Decathlon Long Jump, 400-meter Semi-Final, Decathlon Shot Put, 5,000-meter Final, Decathlon High Jump, 400-meter Final, Decathlon 400-meter

▲ Seventh Day (July 7th)

Decathlon High Hurdles, Decathlon Discus, 400-meter Relay Preliminary, Decathlon Pole Vault, Women's 400-meter Relay Preliminary, 3,000-meter Steeplechase Final, Decathlon Javelin, 1,600-meter Relay Preliminary, Decathlon 1,500-meter

▲ Eighth Day (July 8th)

Women's High Jump Final, 400-meter Relay Semi-Final, Women's 400-meter Relay Final, Cross-Country Race, 400-meter Relay Final, 1,600-meter Relay Final

In addition, the schedule of ball games and other events will be announced after the registration of all countries is completed. Our country sent a representative, Mr. Song Ruhai, to participate in the 9th session. This session should be prepared as soon as possible. The Japanese side will invite American players to the country for competition next year, and then select the elite of the country for a long-term joint training, preparing to make a fierce fight on the world stage.

The competition schedule tonight has two matches, both in Group B.

▲ Youai Wins Fushi (B1)

The battle between Youai and Fushi was the opening act of this tournament. Fushi led with a neat lineup. Youai resisted repeatedly, but still found it difficult to escape the danger. They were behind 10 to 14 in the first half. The situation tightened in the second half. Youai used their lively bodies and agile passing, and progressed step by step. In the last five minutes, relying on Zheng Zhifang's goal, they jumped to the forefront with a score of 16 to 15. Fushi's ambition was still there, and they continued to fight. Soon, Ren Tongyao scored a goal, leading by another point. At this time, the two sides were at a critical moment of life and death, and they all dealt with it with all their attention. Then, Youai's luck was high, and Wan Ruiding was seen shooting a goal, resulting in Youai winning 19 to 18. Referee Fu Hua.

Guangdong Women's Table Tennis Team Reorganization and Expansion

▲Seeking New Comrades, Retaining Zeng as Instructor

The Shanghai Guangdong Women's Table Tennis Team is organized by female comrades in the Guangdong overseas sports community. Its purpose is to promote indoor sports for women during amateur holidays. Since its establishment, it has been nearly a year. Its past work achievements have been deeply praised by Chinese and foreign women in the Shanghai sports community. Talented players such as Ma Baokun, Lin Muzhao, Zheng Lihua, Li Ruifen, Feng Xiaoji, Wei Peiyun, Lin Ruyi, Lin Murong, Zhang Runzhu, Chen Yongbao, Li Guilian, etc., are outstanding table tennis talents gathered from Shanghai's Liangjiang Women's Physical Education College, Fudan University, Guangdong Middle School, Qixiu Girls' School, and Guangzhao Girls' School. Previously, due to busy schoolwork, they had no time to take care of both, and resigned more than three months ago. The team's work has been affected.
