Local News

Record of the Canadian Business Delegation's Inspection Yesterday

▲Tour of the City in the Morning ▲Visit to Factories in the Afternoon ▲Luncheon at the British Chamber of Commerce

▲Welcome by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 4:00 PM ▲Arrival at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 7:00 PM ▲Guests and Hosts Exchanging Speeches

The Canadian Far East Business Delegation arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and was warmly welcomed by all sectors. Yesterday morning, all members of the delegation took cars to tour Shanghai city for a week. At 12:00 noon, they attended a luncheon hosted by the British Chamber of Commerce. After 1:00 PM, they visited major factories. At 4:00 PM, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce held a tea party at Chen's residence, No. 6 Seymour Road, to welcome them. At 7:00 PM in the evening, they attended a banquet hosted by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. It was also decided that they would continue to visit major factories in the city this morning, attend a luncheon hosted by the Pan-Pacific Association at 12:00 noon, and take a ship to Hong Kong at 2:30 PM in the afternoon, with a planned stay of two weeks before returning home. The situation yesterday is recorded as follows:

▲Reception by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce The Municipal Chamber of Commerce hosted a public banquet for the Canadian Business Delegation to China last night. Chairman Wang Xiaolai delivered a speech as follows: Gentlemen of the Canadian Chamber of Commerce Business Delegation, this time you have come from afar, first to Japan, then to China, for a large-scale commercial inspection. In the history of Sino-Canadian trade, this seems to be the first time. My colleagues at the Chamber of Commerce, as the hosts, are extremely welcoming, and we have two feelings about the arrival of these distinguished guests: (1) It is sufficient to prove the drastic changes in the world economy after the European War. Whether it is a country with a small land and a dense population, or a country with abundant products and extremely advantageous geographical conditions, it must open up new markets overseas in order to solve the problem of overproduction and the problem of worker unemployment to a considerable extent. (2) To feel the importance of China and Japan on the Pacific Ocean to the world economy, and comparing the situations of China and Japan one by one, it seems that China is more important to the world economic relationship than Japan. Because, first, China's 400 million population, if its purchasing power is properly developed, is no less than a ratio of 7 to 1 compared to Japan's 60 million population. Secondly, Japan is now an industrial country, and its products are spread all over the world market, with the possibility of competing for hegemony. China, on the other hand, is in the construction era and lacks raw materials and industrial products, which are more needed than any other country. It welcomes the assistance of friendly countries in terms of materials. But if any country in the world can give the Chinese people a friendly attitude and sincere sympathy, then China is willing to recognize it as a mutually beneficial country at any time and quickly abandon narrow-minded views on race. Therefore, my colleagues at the Chamber of Commerce would like to tell you, gentlemen, with a straightforward view that China is the only country in the world that can truly implement the open-door policy, and China is also the only country that can implement economic mutual assistance. Even in terms of the world's current tariff system, almost all countries use tariff policies as a barrier to protect industry. However, since the abolition of the tariff agreement system in China, its revised import tariff rate still maintains an extremely fair and tolerant policy. This advantage is also unique in the world. Therefore, my Chamber of Commerce sincerely hopes that you, the delegation, must first recognize China's position in the world economy, which is more important than that of Japan, in order to achieve the purpose of this visit to China. After recognizing the importance of China's position in the world economy, the second step is to implement the four characters of economic mutual assistance, correct the mistakes of the past history of China and Canada, so as to win the sincere sympathy of the Chinese people and make the commerce between the two countries flourish day by day. There is an old saying in our country: "Those who love others are always loved by others, and those who respect others are always respected by others." It also says, "It is impolite to go without coming, and it is impolite to come without going." My Chamber of Commerce uses these two sentences as an explanation of economic mutual assistance, and I feel that it is still appropriate. The current situation in your country is not comparable to the initial development of industry in the past. There is no need to recruit Chinese workers, and our country's workers do not hope to continue to enter the country. However, my Chamber of Commerce dares to represent the people of the whole country and put forward the fairest and most frank request, which has two main points: (1) For the people of China and Japan entering the country, they should be treated equally, and no special immigration regulations should be set up for China. (2) Since the trade relations between the two countries have not been interrupted, the hub for trade is actually the merchant. Merchants should be absolutely free to come and go. In terms of the principle of equal national relations, merchants from your country who come to our country to do business are not restricted by the amount of capital or the number of years of operation. However, your country restricts our country's merchants from importing unless they have a capital of more than 2,500 Canadian dollars and have been engaged in business for more than three years, and only those who specialize in transporting and selling Sino-Canadian local products in China and Canada are qualified. This kind of restriction is unprecedented in the history of trade between countries. Just imagine that the goods sold in your country's territory are not limited to those produced in China and Canada. Commodities from third countries are not prohibited items. Why can't Chinese merchants be allowed to transport them freely? This approach not only restricts trade, but is tantamount to prohibiting trade. Therefore, according to reports from overseas Chinese businessmen there, recently, no matter how strong the capital of Chinese businessmen entering Canada is, they are generally not recognized for import. Those who are already in Canada are also often subject to the local government's anti-Chinese harshness, such as prohibiting Chinese restaurants from employing white women as waitresses, and factories are not allowed to employ Chinese workers. Judging from their intentions, it seems that they want to gradually reduce all Chinese businesses in Canada. To put it bluntly, it is no different from wanting to turn mutually beneficial commerce into one-sided commerce. This is not an arbitrary empty talk from my Chamber of Commerce. As evidenced by the fact that since your country promulgated 43 immigration regulations in 1923, only four Chinese people have been granted special permission to reside there in the past seven years. In terms of imported and exported goods, in 1929, Chinese goods entering Canada were only 3 million US dollars, while in the same year, Canadian goods entering China were 23.5 million US dollars. This policy of supporting the development of one-sided commerce seems to have achieved considerable success. But can this kind of success continue to develop? Can it be without obstacles? My Chamber of Commerce believes that there is really doubt. Because the Chinese nation is a nation rich in emotion. Decades ago, the motto "Those who love others are always loved by others, and those who respect others are always respected by others" has been widely printed and imprinted in the minds of ordinary people. The era of forcing trade with gunboats has long passed. Therefore, the general public's welcome or rejection of international commerce will naturally shift according to the attitude of the other party. Therefore, anyone who holds narrow-minded views, wants to develop their one-sided commerce, and disregards the feelings of the other party, this kind of policy, if you want it to be permanently smooth and not fail, is just like the ancient saying in our country, "going south by driving the chariot north". My Chamber of Commerce knows that the mistakes in the past history of China and Canada were caused by narrow-minded politicians who wanted to please the public's psychology. But the politicians created the cause, and your country's commerce with China will reap the consequences in the future. Therefore, merchants really have the responsibility to correct it. In the past, the famous people of your country's commercial organizations did not set foot on Chinese soil, and did not know the situation in our country. There was no opportunity to have an open and honest direct meeting, so it is a pity that they allowed politicians to create many mistakes. This visit of your delegation is actually an excellent opportunity to reform the friendship between the peoples of China and Canada. Therefore, I hope that your delegation will not only pay attention to how to expand sales and how to improve commodities, but should understand the sincere attitude and earnest wishes of the Chinese people, and faithfully report what you have learned to your country's authorities and the entire people, and put forward a fair proposal to abolish the special immigration regulations for China and follow the current approach with Japan to sign a mutually beneficial commercial treaty with China. This is the best contribution and the best achievement of your delegation after returning home. My Chamber of Commerce knows that today's remarks are inevitably too straightforward. But when we make friends, we must say everything we know and say everything we can in order to show the sincerity of our friendship. Since your delegation is a good friend of my Chamber of Commerce, we should not hide anything about the permanent interests of the commerce between the two countries. Therefore, I have made a lengthy contribution during this precious time. I hope you will understand. Although the wine and dishes prepared by my Chamber of Commerce today are very simple, the feelings are very sincere. I would like to offer a toast to wish your delegation a successful mission and good health to everyone present.

▲Mr. Ye Mulei's Reply Briefly said that since arriving in Shanghai for two days, we have been entertained repeatedly. The members of my delegation express their gratitude. I also represent the Canadian government and offer its blessings. When we set off, the Prime Minister of Canada was in the United Kingdom, but he sent a telegram expressing his deep interest in my delegation and entrusted me to represent goodwill to the countries I visited. The Minister of Commerce of Canada has the same expression. I also represent the General Chamber of Commerce organized by 205 city chambers of commerce in Canada to greet you. We are pleased to meet an important meeting in Nanjing during our visit to China. Although we have only been here for two days, the Canadian government will definitely make a strong contribution by reporting what we have seen and heard to the Canadian government. Trade between Canada and China has developed greatly in recent years. Before 1914, the highest amount of trade was 750,000 taels. In the past five years, it has increased to 60 million taels. China was Canada's 23rd largest customer in the past, but has jumped to 8th place in the past eight years. Canada's history is only 533 years. The current race has only lived there for 327 years. At that time, they only lived in a small area along the Atlantic coast. It was only 140 years ago that Canadians first went west to the Pacific coast. Sixty years ago, the population of western Canada was less than 100,000. The initial development of our country began 25 years ago. The characteristic of that time was the development of the vast land of western Canada. After the European War, it was followed by a period of construction. In 1924, the greatest development in Canadian history began. As a result, Canada jumped to the fifth place in the world's import and export commerce. Analytically speaking, Canada's new position is fifth in imports and third in exports. Our country's foreign trade in 1929 was 750 million taels, which is about 100 million taels more than in 1900. Agriculture is still the basic industry of Canada and is also its main export. In 1929, we transported and sold 240 million taels of agricultural products abroad, and the land of production in 1929 was only one-fifth of the current land. Forests are Canada's second new source of wealth, and there has also been amazing development in recent years. Planted forests account for more than one-third of Canada's land. Canada's mineral resources are particularly rich. Last year, the value of mineral resources was 90 million taels. Hydroelectric power is also a natural resource developed in Canada after 1925. Canada's fisheries are also a major wealth. The fisheries profit in 1928 was 165 million taels. In addition, Canada's industry has invested 1500 million taels, and the annual output reaches 1000 million taels. The mission of our trip is to promote the common development of commerce between China and Canada.

▲Tea Party at the Two Organizations Zhao Xien, Director of the Industrial and Commercial Visiting Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and Chen Shiguang, Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, specially represented the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and held a tea party at Chen's residence, No. 6 Seymour Road, yesterday afternoon to welcome the Canadian Far East Commercial Inspection Delegation. All members of the delegation attended the meeting. More than 100 guests attended the meeting, including Gu Weijun, Wu Yunzhai, Xu Xinliu, Yuan Ludeng, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, and commercial counselors from various countries. Liu Yunfang, Ye Muji, Tang Shixuan, and Mrs. Chen Bingqian from the Foreign Affairs Office served as hosts. First, they visited the carved screen of Empress Dowager Cixi and famous paintings of the Qing Dynasty displayed in Chen's residence, and then took photos and had tea. The guests and hosts dispersed happily at about 6:00 PM. The tea and snacks yesterday were contracted by Guanshengyuan and were purely Chinese style. Each member of the delegation was also given a can of famous tea as a souvenir.

Recent Situation of Sino-Russian Commercial Transportation

▲A Lot of Fish and Wood Imported ▲Chinese Ships Waiting for Orders in Vladivostok

▲Chartered Ships Released Back to Shanghai Since the resumption of Sino-Russian navigation, the Soviet Russian commercial fleet, because the goods of the Russian Northern Coastal State must be shipped out before the winter freezing period and transferred to China and other places, entrusted British merchants, Laisi Yangxing in Shanghai, to charter more than 30 Chinese, Norwegian, British and other ships in Shanghai to go to the Russian Northern Coastal State to transport sea products, timber and other goods. Most of the charter periods are half a year. Now the climate in Northern Russia is already extremely cold. Among the chartered ships transporting goods in the Coastal State, except for a few British ships with strong quality and young age, the Chinese ships Minghe Wuyang, Daxing, and Fengxiang, according to telegrams, have all returned to Vladivostok, and the Norwegian ships Haifola Tuo, Pilan Ente, French ship Kaman Ensite, Hai Enlv Fulei, and Mang Nasi Tuo have been released back to Shanghai first. Each ship is fully loaded with Russian wood, wool and other goods to Shanghai. The other ships that have arrived in Vladivostok also have news of returning to Shanghai.

▲Large Quantities of Sea Products Arrive in Shanghai Among Russian sea products, salted fish is the largest import to China. It has not come for many years. After the two countries resumed commercial transportation this year, the fish produced in the Coastal State of that country began to be sold to China again in early autumn. Shanghai is sold by Anli and other companies as agents. From autumn to now, more than ten batches of Russian fish have arrived in Shanghai, transported by Japanese merchant ships and Laisi and other ships. The cost of the fish is estimated to be 2.34 million yuan. Shipments have temporarily stopped.

▲Wooden Boats Continue to Arrive Russian Northern forests are extraordinarily rich, and the quality of timber is superior to that of Japanese and American goods. This year, after Russian goods can be transported to Shanghai, a lot of timber has been imported. In the beginning, the materials shipped were mostly raw materials for matchsticks, but recently, what has been shipped are planks, which are much smoother than American wood. There are still two shipments being loaded by the Mang Nasi Tuo and other ships and are being unloaded. It is said that more than ten ships of goods can be transported to Shanghai this year.

▲Chinese Tea Awaiting Shipment to Russia The route for Chinese tea to Russia is huge. After the Soviet Russian Assistance Society came to Shanghai to resume the tea agency this year, it started to purchase tea leaves. In the beginning, it processed tea bricks, but now it only purchases black and green tea to transport to Russia. There are still more than 40,000 boxes of tea that have been purchased in Shanghai and have not been shipped, waiting for the Vladivostok ship to arrive before loading. It is said that the amount of Chinese tea transported to Russia this year is not as much as last year. The reasons are: (1) The Assistance Society resumed later, and most of the bulk goods were purchased by British merchants. (2) The price of tea leaves is higher than last year. Due to these two reasons, it cannot be purchased in large quantities.

▲Regular Liner Still Not Opened British merchants Laisi Yangxing is the authorized representative of Soviet Russian commercial ships in China. All shipping matters are handled by the company. The owner, Ma Le, had planned to open a regular Shanghai-Vladivostok route and resume formal Sino-Russian navigation. He had personally gone to Vladivostok to negotiate with the Soviet Russian authorities. Later, because the commodity trade between China and Russia had not fully recovered, and the number of passengers coming and going could not return to the original state, the four regular liners had been planned but had not yet been implemented. It is now learned that they will wait until the thaw next spring before they can be realized.

The Shanghai Public Concession Water Company, because of the price increase issue, aroused opposition from Chinese and foreign citizens. Water Rate Hike and Water Cut-Off Issue

▲ A Citizen's Letter ▲ The Taxpayers' Association's Statement

The Shanghai Ratepayers' Association of the Foreign Settlement received a letter yesterday from Mr. Wu Fei, a citizen (staff member of the Shanghai Municipal Party Department), which stated: "Respectfully, regarding the Public Utilities Waterworks Company's unreasonable increase in water rates, it has been consistently opposed by both Chinese and Western residents. Your association has also negotiated with the company and stated that before the company's account investigation is completed and the price increase is deemed necessary, the original rate should still be charged. However, the company disregarded your association's statement. I am also a resident within the settlement (on Dalian Bay Road, near Baikal Road). I received a written warning from the company, stating that I must pay the increased water rate immediately. If I do not comply with the increased payment, the water supply will be cut off. Before the case is resolved, I cannot pay according to the increased rate and must wait for your association's negotiation to resolve the matter before proceeding. Water is an essential element of citizens' lives and cannot be lacking for even a day. The settlement authorities do not allow citizens to form a second water company to operate this business, nor do they allow citizens to obtain other water sources for self-sufficiency. Now, the company uses its power to monopolize this public utility, oppresses citizens, unreasonably increases water prices, and threatens to cut off water as a means of coercion. This is truly strangling people to obtain their wealth. But in terms of reason, it is unfair. The matter concerns the vital interests of citizens. I hope that your association will take the interests of citizens as a prerequisite and strive to negotiate with the company to achieve the cancellation of the water rate increase plan. Then, the citizens within the settlement will all look forward to it." The association immediately replied, stating: "Regarding your letter of November 11th, we have received it. Your views on the Shanghai Waterworks Company's price increase are greatly appreciated. Our association will actively negotiate in accordance with public opinion. We have replied accordingly and hope you will provide further guidance."

Central Exchange Certificate Cashing Issue

▲ Joint Request by Certificate Holders for Redemption

During the Northern Expedition in the 15th year of the Republic of China, the Commander-in-Chief of the National Revolutionary Army presented to the National Government and entrusted the General Political Department and Treasury of the Headquarters to issue 5 million yuan of temporary exchange certificates from the Central Bank. The certificates were divided into three denominations: one yuan, five yuan, and ten yuan. The certificates were stamped with the seal of the Commander-in-Chief of the National Revolutionary Army and the official seals of the Director of the General Political Department and the Director of the Treasury. The regulations were formulated and promulgated by the Headquarters, and a proclamation was issued to inform the public of its circulation in the market, and it was fully used. The exchange certificates once circulated in Shanghai, but then suddenly stopped being cashed. Certificate-holding merchants and residents repeatedly appealed to the Ministry of Finance to redeem them. It was instructed to wait for reorganization.

Page 10

case. Now, all certificate holders believe that the Internal and External Debt Reorganization Committee has been meeting in the capital. They all believe that the issuance of the certificates was greatly beneficial to the Northern Expeditionary Army, and the government has the necessity to first reorganize and fully redeem them. Yesterday, they specially organized a joint association of certificate holders and requested Chairman Chiang, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance to consider the difficulties of the merchants and immediately redeem them. They also sent letters to various groups such as the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to appeal. They also plan to publicly elect representatives to petition in Beijing. Also, the holders of the 9 million National Treasury Bonds issued by the Ministry of Finance of the National Government on June 30th of the 16th year of the Republic of China have a similar organization and request.

Wu Song River Shallow Water and Yuji Pier Blockage of Ships

Since the beginning of autumn in this port, the weather has been unusually dry, resulting in very shallow water in rivers everywhere. Small streams and ponds in the countryside have even dried up and become silted. For example, the Suzhou River (i.e., the Wu Song River) was originally an important route in this port, where merchant ships gathered to travel to and from. It reaches Wu Song and the Yangtze River in the east, and Suzhou and Wuxi and even Jiangning in the west. However, due to the narrow river surface in sections such as Zhoujiaqiao North Xinjing Yuji Pier in western Shanghai, ship blockages often occur when the water is shallow, and there is a risk of traffic disruption. Although the Dredging Bureau and the rice and shipping industries have repeatedly met to raise funds for dredging to facilitate traffic, the amount of money is quite large, and work has not yet started. Now, due to the sunny weather in recent days, merchant ships of various industries come and go to load and transport goods, one after another, day and night. It is especially crowded when the tide comes. At about 3:30 yesterday morning, a ship blockage suddenly occurred in the Yuji Pier area west of North Xinjing in northwestern Shanghai, and traffic was completely cut off. At first, there were about a hundred cargo ships, etc. As it got lighter, there were more and more at both ends of the east and west. By noon, there were about eight or nine hundred, extending for several miles. Among them, rice boats and vegetable boats were the most numerous. Even the small steamboats from Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, and Changshu Dangkou to Shanghai were all blocked in the boats, and the passengers were trapped in the boats. Even the rice market in Zhabei was short of rice boats. It is heard that the water patrol team and the first branch of the sixth district have sent police to try to dredge, but due to the large number of ships, it is difficult to arrange them at once. By the evening, it was still blocked, so the small steamboats of the North Suzhou Road Lao Gongmao Merchants and other steamboat bureaus to Suzhou, Wuxi, and Changshu Dangkou temporarily returned all the passenger tickets sold and stopped running, temporarily suspending one shift.

Various Labor Unions Assist Labor Unions in Maintaining Organizations

Requesting the Fourth Plenary Session to Enact Separate Regulations for Labor Unions

The various labor unions in this city, in view of the fact that the national labor unions are requesting to maintain permanent organizations, sent representatives to the Fourth Plenary Session to petition, and went to great lengths to appeal. Specially, in view of the friendship of sympathy, they unanimously advocated assistance and petitioned the Fourth Plenary Session on their behalf. Now, the original text of the joint petition of the various labor unions is recorded below,

The petition is to request permission for workers to maintain permanent organizations and to enact separate regulations for workers' unions, in order to emphasize the movement of the people. Since the banner of the Blue Sky with a White Sun flew over Southeast China, workers' unions in various places have sprung up. Major ones such as driving out warlords and supporting the revolution, and minor ones such as improving skills and developing businesses, have become a strong and legitimate people's organization. Unexpectedly, after the Blue and White banner had been flying across the country for a long time, the Legislative Yuan enacted the Law of Industrial and Commercial Guilds and the Implementing Regulations of Guilds, which completely shaken the organization of workers' unions across the country from the root. Although representatives of the workers' unions were publicly elected and went to Beijing to petition, they were graciously granted permission to postpone the cancellation. However, due to the fact that separate regulations have not been enacted, there is a fear that they will disappear like the evening sun and morning dew. The millions of workers across the country will inevitably lose their guarantee. The members of the association belong to the same level and share weal and woe. They dare to present the reasons why the organization of workers' unions must be permanently maintained to your association in detail. It is believed that the party's doctrine first emphasizes assisting people's organizations, so those who are truly loyal to the party and the country must maintain the established people's organizations. Those that have not been established should be guided in every possible way to establish them. This is the responsibility that those who seek to implement the doctrine should fulfill. Now, workers' unions are a group that has been established for many years, and they not only have a sound organization, but also a glorious history. Instead of supporting them, they are allowed to disappear. According to the party's doctrine, this is clearly contrary to it. This is for the sake of implementing the party's doctrine, and the organization of workers' unions must be permanently maintained. Second, the development of the people's movement lies in expanding the implementation of civil rights as much as possible, especially the promotion of universal suffrage. The Implementing Regulations of Guilds stipulate that only when there are more than fifteen workers can one representative be elected to join the guild. It is found that our country's assets are backward. Not only are there no large stores in the interior, but even in large cities that can employ more than fifteen workers, it is feared that they can be counted on one's fingers. If there is no corresponding liaison agency, it will be a piece of loose sand. The procedures for election cannot be implemented, and opinions will be divided. How can reforms be sought regarding their own interests? Under the guise of merging, the reality of elimination is carried out. As a result, it will inevitably make millions of workers who can truly participate in the people's movement and exercise their rights as sparse as morning stars, hindering the people's movement and depriving civil rights. The purpose of the prime minister's efforts to revolutionize should not be so. This is for the sake of developing the people's movement and civil rights, and the organization of workers' unions must be permanently maintained. The positions of labor and capital are equal, and there are many things that are in their common interests, but when interests conflict, it will inevitably be inevitable. With workers' unions buffering in between, when the capital side exerts pressure horizontally, it can make earnest appeals on behalf of the labor side, and when the labor side makes unreasonable trouble, it can make detailed explanations on behalf of the capital side. Eliminating disputes is the best way to do this. Now, all workers' unions will be cancelled, and representatives of store clerks, who are as sparse as morning stars, will join the guild. No matter how small the amount, it will not help, and the crowd will inevitably be at the mercy of the capital side. Millions of workers will not be guaranteed for a long time. The consequences of the horizontal decision can be very dangerous. This is for the sake of eliminating labor-capital disputes, and the organization of workers' unions must be permanently maintained. In short, workers' unions are people's organizations that have been established for many years, with organization and history. Now that the period of political tutelage has begun, and we are urgently seeking to complete the construction, it is appropriate to support them to reach the realm of growth and prosperity. Under no circumstances should we cut our feet to fit the shoes and allow them to return to the position of listening to the life and death of the capital side a dozen years ago. The members of the association belong to the same labor force, and they dare not risk being presumptuous. They earnestly request that your association examine and approve the permanent organization of workers' unions and quickly enact separate regulations for workers' unions for compliance. The people's movement is fortunate, and the party and the country are fortunate. Presenting this petition, we are eagerly awaiting orders. Sincerely presented to the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang.

All Sectors Discussed and Decided on Measures to Promote the National Calendar New Year

▲ Revised and Approved Based on the Principles Decided Last Time

The measures for promoting the National Calendar New Year in this city were previously discussed and decided by all sectors convened by the Social Affairs Bureau, and the principles were approved on record. It is now heard that the meeting, in order to strive for careful consideration, after the principles were approved at the last meeting, five people including Chen Kecheng, Zhang Zhenyuan, and Zheng Chengqing were appointed as examiners to re-examine the entire plan. It has recently been completed. Yesterday afternoon, another meeting was held in the Social Affairs Bureau, and more than 20 representatives from all sectors attended. As a result of the meeting, it has been revised and approved based on the review report, and it has been submitted to the municipal government today for approval, and then distributed to various agencies for execution. The revised measures are excerpted below,

▲ (1) Submitting to the Municipal Government for Promulgation (Zi)

During the twelfth month of the lunar calendar, those who sell or carry stove god sedan chairs or pedestrians will be confiscated by the patrol police at any time. (Chou) From February 1st to the end of February, it is forbidden to set off firecrackers, flower tubes, shooting stars, etc. Violators will be detained and fined. (Yin) Ancestral sacrifices, New Year's Eve dinner, and spring banquets will all be changed to be held at the end of the year and the beginning of the year according to the national calendar. (Mao) It is stipulated that January 5th is the opening day. Order the Chamber of Commerce to notify everyone. If the God of Wealth is respected at the beginning of the lunar calendar, the police station may ban it and impose a small fine as appropriate. (Chen) It is forbidden to open temples on New Year's Eve of the lunar calendar. (Ji) Allow all sectors to hold a Lantern Festival celebration on January 15th, playing New Year's gongs and drums, and parading in the streets. Lantern vendors and paper shops are allowed to sell lanterns during the National Calendar New Year. It is absolutely forbidden to play gongs and drums or parade at the beginning of the lunar calendar, and lantern vendors and paper shops are forbidden to sell lanterns, etc. Violators will be confiscated. (Wu) Re-promulgate the instructions of the Executive Yuan No. 3987 to close accounts at the end of the year. (Wei) From January 1st to 4th is the New Year's holiday. Those with original customary holidays that exceed this number may refer to and move them to the end of the year and the beginning of the year according to the national calendar. (Such as the dyeing industry sealing the vat and the food industry opening. It is strictly forbidden to take holidays at the beginning and end of the lunar calendar under the name of the Spring Festival or other names. Violators will be ordered to open for business by the police station and will be responsible for notifying the Chamber of Commerce and the same industry association in advance. (Shen) The closing of theaters and the closure of amusement parks and restaurants for repairs are all allowed to be carried out at the end of the year according to the national calendar, but they should all be open for business in the New Year to allow the public to enjoy themselves, and the police station will inform them. (You) Year-end double salaries and annual bonuses should also be changed to be issued according to the national calendar. (Xu) All shops in the city should move the year-end cleaning of the lunar calendar to December 15th according to the national calendar.

(2) ▲ To be executed by the Public Security Bureau (Jia) The district office should notify the matters to be banned at the end of the year and the beginning of the year in advance, and the relevant industries will execute them when the time comes. (Yi) In conjunction with the concession police station, search and destroy old lunar calendars and widely persuade people to buy the calendar compiled and printed by this city.

▲ (3) To be handled by the Municipal Party Department (Jia) Notify all newspapers that they are not allowed to publish New Year advertisements during the Lunar New Year. (Yi) Proclaim to all sectors of the public that the name of the Spring Couplets should be changed to New Couplets, and they are only allowed to be posted during the National Calendar New Year. The couplets will be compiled and promulgated by the Municipal Propaganda Department. (Bing) The People's Training Committee should notify the printing workers' union and the newspaper delivery workers' union in advance that they must not stop work at the beginning and end of the lunar calendar. (Ding) Supervise the various district branches under its jurisdiction to make every effort to promote the National Calendar New Year to the public, such as open-air speeches, and print and paste slogans, and distribute simple vernacular texts and pictures to persuade them. (Wu) If any workers' union protects or is not enthusiastic about promoting the National Calendar New Year, the People's Training Committee will punish it. The punishment measures will be formulated and promulgated by the People's Training Committee.

▲ (4) To be jointly reviewed and handled by the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau Proclaim to the workers of various factories that if they take a holiday at the beginning of the Lunar New Year, if the initiative comes from the capital side, the wages of the shop assistants and workers will be doubled on a daily basis. If it comes from the workers, their wages will also be doubled on a daily basis.

▲ (5) To be executed by the Education Bureau (Jia) Order all schools to publicize the measures for promoting the National Calendar New Year to students and their families as soon as possible. (Yi) Prevent teachers and students from taking leave from February 10th to the end of February unless they have illness or important matters. Violators will be punished. (Bing) Select cadres to conduct strict investigations in various schools at the beginning of the lunar calendar.

▲ (6) To be reviewed and handled by the Postal and Telecommunications Bureau (Jia) Write to the Telegraph Bureau to give special convenience to New Year's telegrams during the National Calendar and stop sending Lunar New Year's telegrams. (Yi) Write to the Post Office to stop sending Lunar New Year's postcards.

▲ (7) To be handled by the newspaper industry (Jia) Disclose the documents promoting the National Calendar New Year as much as possible. (Yi) Journalists should write texts and pictures to promote the significance of promoting the National Calendar New Year and abolishing the old calendar. (Bing) Various newspapers should not stop publishing at the beginning of the lunar calendar.

(8) Regarding party and government agencies (Jia) In addition to executing the above-mentioned matters in their respective positions, all party and government personnel should set an example by themselves. Violators will be punished separately according to their discipline. (Yi) The New Year holidays for various agencies, including commemorative days, are only three days. At the beginning of the promotion, they should submit a request to the municipal government and write to the Municipal Party Department to allow holidays from December 30th to January 4th to arouse social attention and promote the concept of attaching importance to the National Calendar. And for the sake of closing accounts, civil servants are not without family affairs to deal with. This year-end and beginning-of-year holiday should be extended as appropriate.

▲ (9) Write to the Secretariat of the Municipal Government for review and handling

to print the measures for promoting the National Calendar New Year in a simple and large size, such as leaflets, and print 400,000 copies to be distributed door-to-door by the various districts of the Public Security Bureau at the beginning of December so that everyone knows and has preparations. ▲ (10) Regarding the celebration ceremony, submit to the municipal government for instructions

(1) New Year's family ceremony, A, New Year's Eve is a memorial to ancestors, gathering family members, young and old, to offer incense and flowers, and hang a portrait of ancestors in the middle hall. The memorial ceremony is as follows: 1. Stand at attention, 2. Bow to the ancestors, 3. The head of the family offers flowers, 4. Report (explain the significance of the memorial, so that they know what they have experienced in the year and instruct the ancestors' portraits, and describe their legacy and anecdotes that are worthy of instruction), 5. Perform the year-end ceremony (the younger generation bows to the head of the family), 6. Family feast (2) New Year's Day celebration ceremony, 1. Stand at attention, 2. Salute the party and the national flag and the Prime Minister's portrait, 3. Bow to the ancestors, 4. The head of the family speaks (explains the significance of the New Year's celebration, and must make them know that the New Year begins to work hard in learning and career, and encourage family members) 5. Perform the New Year's ceremony (the younger generation performs the New Year's ceremony to the head of the family and the respected members), 6. Give gifts (the head of the family rewards the younger generation with money, food, stationery) 7. Feast, 8. Other entertainment, submit to the municipal government for audit and handling. The reviewers of the above cases are Zhang Zhenyuan, Chen Kecheng, Zhang Yaoming, and Zheng Chengqing.

Shipping News

▲ Xinfeng Returns to Shanghai for Repairs The Zhaoshang Bureau's Beiyang liner Xinfeng was damaged by a Japanese ship in Tianjin, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, the ship returned to Shanghai and docked at the Jinliyuan Wharf to unload cargo. It will enter the factory for major repairs today. According to the crew of the ship, the Xinfeng was about one mile away from Tianjin Zizhu Forest at about 5:00 pm on the 8th of this month, at a place called Yangzhuangzi. It was high tide at the time, and the Xinfeng was sailing in with the current. The bow of the ship was lit up with a green light as usual. The Japanese ship Jingshan Maru was going out at this time against the current. According to the navigation regulations, the ship against the current should give way to the ship with the current. Unexpectedly, the Japanese ship did not give way, resulting in a disaster in which the two ships met and collided with each other. The upper deck and three sampans of the Xinfeng were all crushed and destroyed, and the keel was bent and the hull's 25 ribs were also damaged. The responsibility was entirely borne by the Japanese ship. Yesterday, Captain Ma Xun of the Xinfeng reported to the General Bureau. After the engineering department sent engineers to inspect the ship, it will enter the dry dock for major repairs after unloading the incoming cargo. Today, Yushun is temporarily ordered to take over the shift, and negotiations have been launched with the Japanese Post Coastal Society to claim compensation for losses.

▲ Tongyang New Ship Sails The Dayuan Shipping Bureau, a new company in the Tongyang line, has been preparing for a long time, and it is now ready. The routes and wharves have all been taken care of. At first, the Fushun ship was rented from Wenxing Company to run this line. Later, because the Fushun's draft was 17 feet, it could not run. It has now been returned to Wenxing, and two other ships, Yu'an (900 tons) and Da'an (850 tons), have been rented and sent to Tongyang. In Shanghai, Wharf No. 10 in Nanshi has been designated as the berth, and it is approved that the Yu'an ship will be sent to open the maiden voyage route on the 29th of this month.

▲ Pier Damaged and Repaired The case of Baohe Shipping Company's Yue Si Bao City ship damaging the Hongkou Pier of the Rich Qing Company and sinking ten private ship cargo barges is now being dealt with by the Rich Qing Company. Because the Yangtze River ships must berth at the pier, the Rich Qing Company has sent craftsmen to repair it. The estimated repair cost is about 20,000 taels. The Rich Qing Company has negotiated with Baohe, demanding that it bear the compensation, and is rushing to repair it. It is expected to be completed today.

▲ Large Batch of Silk and Tea Shipped to the UK Today, the British mail ship Camilla exported 10,000 boxes of Chinese tea purchased by British merchants in this port to London, worth one million yuan, and 500 pieces of Huzhou silk, also worth 600,000 yuan, all shipped out to London by the ship.

Shanghai Municipal Public Utilities Bureau Revises the Measures for Issuing Reduced Price Tickets for Pujiang Ferry

The Shanghai Municipal Public Utilities Bureau issued a notice yesterday, saying, "For notification matters, it is found that Articles 2 and 8 of the Measures for Issuing Free and Half-Price Tickets for Pujiang Ferry in this city have now been revised by the bureau and submitted to the municipal government for approval. The revised articles are hereby notified to the public." Attached is the full text of the revised Articles 2 and 8 of the Measures for Issuing Free and Half-Price Tickets for Pujiang Ferry in this city. "(2) Those who request to issue free tickets are limited to the following agencies that must send people back and forth across the Pujiang River from time to time to take the Pujiang Ferry: (A) all departments and bureaus of this municipal government (affiliated agencies of each department and bureau and)

Each district is limited to those within the scope of the ferry route. ) (B) Other agencies that use municipal funds, type A issues unnamed tickets, but when used, the staff certificate issued by the service agency must be shown, and workers can use symbols instead. Type B issues named tickets, which must be designated by their agency as one representative, and attach the most recent half-length photo of the person, and fill in the position held. (8) Those who hold half-price tickets should first purchase tickets at the ticket office at the pier before boarding the ship with the certificate, and abide by the ferry regulations. If they board the ship without a ticket, regardless of the distance of the route, the half-price ticket will not take effect and they will still have to make up for the ticket according to the cabin position taken and the price set on the ship."

Shanghai Municipal Public Utilities Bureau Revises the Preferential Ticket Measures for Military Police on Ferries

The Shanghai Municipal Public Utilities Bureau yesterday revised the measures for issuing preferential tickets to military police on ferries in this city as follows: (1) This preferential ticket is specially prepared for sale to military police in uniform and wearing official symbols, and those who are not in uniform and do not have official symbols will not be allowed to use it. (2) This preferential ticket is sold for 10 copper coins regardless of the distance of the route, and is limited to one use on the same day. (3) Military police who purchase this preferential ticket can only take the second-class cabin and are not allowed to lie down. If they sit in a cabin beyond their grade, they must still add tickets according to the price set on the ship. (4) Military police on the ship should abide by all the regulations on the ship and listen to the guidance of the crew in case of emergency. (5) Non-military police who falsely purchase this preferential ticket, once found, regardless of the distance of the route, in addition to being ordered to make up for the ticket according to the cabin position taken and the price set on the ship, they will also be fined three times the original price at the ticket office at the pier. (6) Military police who refuse to purchase tickets should have the ferry personnel ask for their name and the military unit and police station they belong to, and record the symbol number and report it to the Public Utilities Bureau and forward it to the competent agency for verification. (7) These measures shall be implemented with the approval of the mayor, and any amendments in the future shall still be subject to the mayor's approval.

Joint Defense News

▲ Chuansha Joins the Four Counties The four counties of Shangsong, Nanfeng, and Fengxian have implemented joint defense for two months. When the last standing committee meeting was held in Shanghai, one of the discussion items was whether Chuansha County should join. It was decided that Shanghai County should write to Chuansha to solicit agreement. Since the letter was sent, a reply was received from the Chuansha County Government yesterday, stating roughly that since the bandits and communists have not yet been eliminated, they should follow the other counties and defend everything. Therefore, the joint defense of the four counties will be changed to the joint defense of the five counties of Shangsong, Nanfeng, Fengxian, and Chuansha. The third standing committee meeting at the end of this month will be held in Nancheng.

▲ Provincial Order for Three Counties and One District The Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department believes that local bandits and parties are rampant and defense is important, and has divided the counties in the province into joint defense zones. The three counties of Songjiang, Shanghai, and Jinshan are in one joint defense zone, and the magistrate of Songjiang County, Jin Qingzhang, is designated as the joint defense director. Magistrate Jin is scheduled to convene a meeting at the Songjiang County Government on the 17th of this month to discuss everything. Therefore, Magistrate Yan of Shanghai County and Secretary Ye Dezhen took the early bus to Songjiang yesterday to attend and discuss the progress together.

▲ The Special Party Headquarters of the Jin-Hu and Hu-Hang-Yong Railways held its 70th Premier's Memorial Week at its auditorium yesterday, the 17th, at 9:00 AM, led by Committee Member Zheng Wenli. After the ceremony, a report was given on major domestic and international events of the past week (omitted), as well as news from the two railways. The railway bureau has purchased eight new buses, four of which have arrived and are being assembled. They are expected to be put into service in about two weeks. The remaining four buses are expected to arrive in Shanghai within the year. After the new locomotives are fully in service, trains will no longer be delayed. In addition, the ferry service between Nanjing and Pukou requires more than 4.4 million yuan in funding and is scheduled to begin construction on December 15. The report concluded and the meeting adjourned.

Funeral of Naval Veteran Lin Baoyi

Naval veteran, Admiral, and former Minister of the Navy Lin Baoyi (Yueqing) passed away on September 14th at his residence on Tongfu Road in the city. A public memorial service was held at Chongfa Temple on Guling Road the day before yesterday. The funeral procession took place at 1:00 PM yesterday, departing from his residence on Tongfu Road and proceeding via Foch Road, Avenue Edward VII, Tibet Road, and Fujian Road before arriving at the International Cemetery on Hongqiao Road for burial. In addition to dispatching a naval band to pay respects, the Ministry of the Navy of the National Government also sent armed marines to carry the funeral rope. The Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau also sent a band to pay respects. Notable figures from the naval community and dignitaries from all walks of life attended and carried the funeral rope. The ceremony was extremely solemn.

Local News II

European Swindler Returned from Japan

▲Swindled Over 10,000 Yuan Worth of Jewelry

▲Intercepted Upon Arrival in Kobe

▲The Person and Stolen Goods Returned to Shanghai the Day Before Yesterday

The American firm Sinlee & Co. on Nanjing Road was swindled out of diamond rings and other jewelry worth over 10,000 yuan by a European on the 31st of last month. The police were notified and requested to investigate. It is now known that the person is of New Lichtenstein nationality, named Heningen, who fled to Japan by ship after obtaining the stolen goods. Upon arrival in Kobe, he was intercepted by local authorities. The General Police Department was notified and dispatched a Western detective to Japan to extradite him. He was returned with the stolen goods the day before yesterday and handed over to the Special District Court yesterday morning. Magistrate Ge conducted the preliminary hearing. Police lawyer Ru Baoyi stated that the defendant had many names. On August 31st, he identified himself as Wulanger from Singapore's Wulanger Jewelry Store, presenting a letter of introduction from the store. Claiming to want to purchase jewelry, Sinlee employees let him choose. He selected a platinum diamond ring worth 8,200 yuan, a platinum watch worth 1,500 yuan, a platinum watch chain worth 240 yuan, a gold cigarette case worth 680 yuan, and a gold pencil worth 690 yuan. He also temporarily took 300 yuan in cash, saying he would return it all on the 2nd of this month. However, he disappeared without a trace. After receiving the report, the police investigated and learned that the swindler's real name was Hetmisk, and he had changed his name again upon leaving Shanghai. The Hui Li police, knowing the ship he was on would pass through Japan, telegraphed Japanese officials to be vigilant and intercept him. Now that he has been apprehended, further investigation is needed. Therefore, a postponement is requested. Magistrate Ge granted the request, ordered the defendant to be detained, and rescheduled the hearing.

Daredevil Corps Leader Extorted 10,000 Yuan

▲Zheng Xirong Recently Received a Threatening Letter

▲Instructed to Deliver Money at the White Cross on the Ground

▲Faced the Riverbank and Made Excuses to Converse

▲Detectives Seized Him When They Emerged from All Directions

Zheng Xirong, manager of the Ronghua Handkerchief Factory in Jiqing Lane, Rue du Consulat, French Concession, recently received a threatening letter demanding 10,000 yuan. The letter was signed by the leader of the Daredevil Corps, surnamed Wang, instructing Zheng to deliver the money at 5:35 PM the day before yesterday to the roadside opposite the morgue on Route Tenant de la Tour. The contact point was a white cross drawn on the ground. The person delivering the money should hold a dry tobacco pipe in his right hand and carry incense and candles in his left hand for identification. If these instructions were ignored, other measures would be taken. After receiving the letter, Zheng reported it to the General Police Department of the International Settlement. The head detective dispatched detectives Ma Xiaozhi, Tian Jinfu, Han Shoushan, and others to the location as scheduled, hiding nearby. Zheng also sent Gu Caiqi to wait at the designated location as instructed in the letter. Soon, a man arrived and lingered for a long time. He then pretended to urinate, facing the riverbank, and said to Gu, "I am Wang, who sent the letter. If you are Zheng's representative, you can hand over the money." At that moment, the detectives who had been lying in ambush all around rushed forward and apprehended him. They took him to the police station. Upon questioning, the bandit's real name was Yu Kanghai, a native of Ningbo. He confessed that he was entrusted by someone to go to the location to make contact and would receive six small silver coins as compensation. The head detective ordered him to be detained. He was sent to the Special District Court yesterday morning. Magistrate Ge conducted the preliminary hearing. According to Yu's confession, he was instructed to go there to make contact and would receive a reward of six small silver dollars. Subsequently, police lawyer Ru Baoyi requested a postponement for investigation. Magistrate Ge then ordered the defendant to be detained and rescheduled the hearing.

Bride Kidnapped

▲Ransom Demand of 15,000 Yuan ▲Unexpectedly Met Her Father on the Way

▲Accompanied by a Man ▲Confessed to Staying in the Same Hotel

Yin Xiumei, a graduate of Ai Qun Girls' School, from Jiangdu, 21 years old, with bright eyes, white teeth, petite and exquisite, is the beloved daughter of Yin Shuqiao, who works at the yarn and cloth exchange. Since childhood, she was betrothed to the son of a wealthy Wu family in Zhenjiang. The wedding was scheduled for the sixth day of the tenth lunar month this year. Yin Shuqiao lived in Shanghai's Zhabei Sanguantang Bridge. Due to his busy business, he was unable to return home immediately. He ordered his beloved daughter, Xiumei, to return to Zhenjiang first to prepare for the wedding. She took a car back home on the sixth day of the ninth lunar month. Her father, Yin Shuqiao, planned to return home closer to the wedding date. Unexpectedly, Xiumei was kidnapped by several burly men only a few days after returning home. Her father received a letter in Shanghai from the First Regiment Headquarters of the Angel Army. The letter stated that his daughter was being treated with courtesy at the regiment. As the regiment was about to depart, they were requesting a loan of 15,000 silver dollars from him to help with their journey. If he complied, his daughter would be returned to his residence immediately. Otherwise, they would have to take legal action. The deadline for the money was the 24th of this month, to be delivered to the Earth God Temple between Qianjiawan and Mabi Lane. After receiving the letter, Yin Shuqiao had no such large sum of money, so he could only comply. He informed the groom's family and changed the wedding date. He secretly searched for and rescued his daughter, hoping to recover his pearl. He then returned to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, at 3:40 PM yesterday (the 17th), his beloved daughter, Yin Xiumei, was walking on Minquan Road Lao Bei Men Xi with an unfamiliar man. Her father, Yin Shuqiao, recognized her and immediately shouted, leading the police Tang Yukun from the Fifth Guard of the Second District First Precinct to arrest the man and woman together and take them to the police station. After questioning by Police Chief Qian, Yin Shuqiao stated the above. The defendant, Jiang Xueguang, 23 years old, from Wusong, who lives in a hotel, confessed that he was friends with Miss Yin Xiumei. Because Xiumei did not want to marry into the Wu family, they discussed and led Xiumei out and sent a letter to her father, requesting a loan of 15,000 yuan. However, he had no intimate relationship with Miss Xiumei. Yin Xiumei confessed that she learned that her parents arranged for her to marry a fiancé surnamed Wu, who was very bad and uneducated, and she feared that it would be difficult to live together as a couple in the future, so she did not want to marry. Because the wedding date was near, she eloped with her friend. She is now staying at a hotel with Jiang Xueguang and denied any intimate relationship. Police Chief Qian believed that the matter involved kidnapping and extortion, and the defendant Jiang Xueguang had already confessed without denial. He ordered them to be handed over to the Public Security Bureau for further investigation to deter illegal activities. Furthermore, Jiang Xueguang works at Huang Yuping's law office and studied at Peking University. He has known Yin Xiumei for many years and they have fallen in love. However, they met more than two years ago. Yin had a friend named Zhao, who lived in the Dahua Apartments in the French Concession. Jiang Xueguang was also acquainted with Zhao. At that time, Yin Xiumei often went to Zhao's place to tutor English and arithmetic, so she met Jiang and became friends. Later, they worked together in a certain party headquarters.

Verdict in Qingyun Lane Demolition Case to be Announced Today

In the Qingyun Lane demolition and assault case, residents of the lane, feeling aggrieved by the illegal oppression they suffered at the hands of Jardine Matheson's comprador Xing Dingcheng, who personally led White Russians in the field to direct the demolition, hired lawyers Wang Zuxun and Xue Jiaqi to file a private prosecution in the Special District Court, seeking redress. Magistrate Cheng Shangfeng presided over the case, which has gone through five court hearings. Due to the importance of the case, the courtroom was unusually crowded with people from all walks of life attending the hearing. The debate has now concluded and the verdict is scheduled to be announced in the Second Criminal Court of the Special District Court at 2:00 PM today (Tuesday).

Li Yanchun's Car Accident Injuring Male and Female Elementary School Students

▲Students' Families File Lawsuit ▲Demanding Compensation for Substantial Losses

Li Yanchun, a traveling salesman for Mobil Oil, drove his private car (Shanghai Municipal Council license plate 10492, Shanghai Municipal Government license plate 5908) at high speed from Dixwell Road to North Szechuan Road on September 19th at 1:00 PM. He suddenly swerved onto the sidewalk, knocking down five male and female elementary school students and shattering the window of Tanaka Barber Shop. The five boys and girls who were hit were returning home for lunch and going to school together. They were walking near Yong An Li on North Szechuan Road when they were hit by Li Yanchun's car and suffered varying degrees of injury. Yang Chunhua, a girl, died from her injuries. Shen Yumei, a girl, fractured the ulna of her right arm. Shen Weiwen, a boy, suffered head and tooth injuries. The two children live at 92 Fengle Lane and are students at Guanghua School. Yang Yingyun, a girl, fractured her left foot bone. Yang Shuying, a girl, fractured her left shoulder bone and suffered a puncture wound to the head, resulting in excessive blood loss. She immediately lost consciousness. The two children live at 91 Scott Road and are students at Guangzhao Public School. The father of the two Yangs is named Yang Mingxin and is currently a customs official at the Longzhou Customs. The father of the two Shens is named Shen Huiru and is the director of the fertilizer department at Brunner, Mond & Co. The victims' families hired a lawyer to file a criminal and civil lawsuit against Li Yanchun in the Special District Court. Yang Mingxin could not come to Shanghai to testify because he was in another location, so he commissioned his relative Yang Sulan to appear in court on his behalf, demanding that Li Yanchun pay maintenance fees of 5,000 taels for Yang Yingyun, 5,000 taels for Yang Shuying, 10,000 taels for Shen Yumei, and 3,000 taels for Shen Weiwen. Medical expenses of 1,200 taels for Yang Yingyun, 300 taels for Yang Shuying, 600 taels for Shen Yumei, and 1,500 taels for Shen Weiwen. The hearing was held in the Special District Court yesterday afternoon at 2:30 PM, presided over by Judge Shen. The defendant, Li Yanchun, claimed that he was returning from fighting a fire that day. Judge Shen said that even if he was fighting a fire, he could not disregard human life. The hearing was scheduled to continue next Monday.

Xin Dingxiang's Family Submits Document to Municipal Public Security Bureau

Xin Dingxiang's family submitted a document to the Municipal Public Security Bureau yesterday, stating that it was submitted regarding the tragic death of Xin Dingxiang and requesting that they negotiate and severely punish the murderer. Xin's son, Dingxiang, was shot by French sailors, fell into the river, and died. They received instructions from the Bureau to have the Marine Police Station summon them to the case. They were also informed that the French Consul General, Genglin, had agreed to strictly detain the sailors involved in the case and ordered them to immediately open a loss sheet for everything after the death, so that they could negotiate compensation with the French Consul General. This showed the Bureau's utmost intention to protect the people, for which they were deeply grateful. However, the most important point in this case was to punish the murderer, and compensation was secondary. Although the French Consul General had stated that the sailors involved in the case would be strictly detained, it was not known which sailors were being punished, or what their names were. Even if the right to judge had not been recovered and they could not be punished according to our country's laws, it should be clearly announced which laws of that country were being cited, so that the truth could be clarified and confusion avoided. The family was deeply saddened by their son's death and had no choice but to plead with the Bureau to negotiate strictly, striving to announce the above details as much as possible and consider the punishment to be commensurate with the crime. Only then would they discuss compensation, otherwise they would not be willing to accept it. They tearfully stated that they could not wait to hear back from the Municipal Public Security Bureau Director Yuan of Shanghai.

Kidnapper You Quan'gen in Liu Nianchun Case Arrested

On Saturday last week, Xinzha Police Detective Zhang Ankang received a tip that You would be going to a restaurant at 39 Fujian Road at 1:00 PM that day for a meal. Unidentified Man Killed by Black Car

Yesterday afternoon around 1:00 PM, an unidentified man wearing a black jacket and trousers, about twenty years old, was walking near Dananmen when a black car suddenly came from the east, speeding west. The man was unable to avoid it and was knocked to the ground, with the car wheels running over his body, causing injuries and bleeding from his nose. He copied down the car's license plate number as 5858. He then took the injured man to Shanghai Hospital for treatment, but he died shortly after arriving at the hospital due to his severe injuries. He immediately reported this to Police Chief Jin, who, considering the matter involved a death, ordered Gu Tiayun, the neighborhood chief of the Twelfth Ward, to report to the Local Court and request an autopsy. Chen A'di was taken to the police station pending investigation by the chief.

▲Seemed to Have a Mental Illness

Yesterday afternoon around 1:00 PM, a Western patrolman from the Marine Police Station was patrolling the Suzhou River by boat when he suddenly saw a teenager jump into the river from the Jiangxi Road Bridge to commit suicide. He immediately took measures to rescue him and took him to the police station. The teenager claimed to be Chen Zaiyou, 19 years old, from Taizhou, but the rest of his words were unclear. He then suffered a mental breakdown, jumping around the police station, crying and laughing, muttering incoherently. Xu Chunrong Detained Due to Shareholding Dispute

Well-known businessman Xu Chunrong and Chen Weirong, Gao Fanglin, Zhu Chenshi and others co-founded Ruishenghe Silk Shop, with Chen as the manager. They had profits for many years. Later, because Xu Chunrong engaged in real estate business, he used the Silk Shop's savings to purchase real estate, causing Ruishenghe's capital turnover to be strained and eventually shut down. Zhu Chenshi hired a lawyer to sue for the division of shares and the distribution of dividends. The court ruled that Xu Chunrong, Chen Weirong, Gao Fanglin, Gao Weiquan, etc., were jointly responsible and should compensate the plaintiff Zhu Chenshi the amount she deserved according to her shares. Xu and others were dissatisfied and repeatedly appealed to the Supreme Court, which was delayed for three years. The final judgment was made this spring and was still enforced according to the original judgment. The Special District Court repeatedly decided to hold a hearing, but Xu and others avoided appearing. Recently, they issued an arrest warrant, ordering the plaintiff to identify and arrest them for execution. After Zhu Chenshi inquired in many ways, she learned that Xu and others often went to Lao Zhenhe Dyeing Shop. So, she went to the dyeing shop with the clerks and police detectives of the Special Court and arrested Xu Chunrong. The executing judge, Xiong Fei, held a court hearing and ordered Xu to be sent to the detention center to be detained, and he would be released after he paid off the debts. It is said that Xu is a native of Shaoxing, and he has many businesses in Shanghai and is good at doing good deeds and has many acquaintances. His friends are now planning to petition the court to demand bail.

Mei Lanfang Special Collection Published

▲Special Sale Starting Today

Mr. Mei Lanfang, the grand master of the Chinese performing arts world, has returned from the United States with an even greater reputation. Some of Mr. Mei's friends have compiled a large special collection, divided into five sections: (1) "Photography of Mei Lanfang and His Family," including recent portraits of Mr. Mei in formal attire, Western suits, and traditional Chinese clothing, as well as recent photographs of Mrs. Fu Zhifang, all extremely valuable and rarely seen by outsiders; (2) "Photography of Mei Lanfang in Costume," including dozens of scenes from "Daiyu Burying Flowers," "A Smile Worth a Thousand Gold," "Farewell My Concubine," "Xi Shi," "Lady Shangyuan," "Magu Presenting Longevity," "Red Thread Stealing the Box," "Mulan Joining the Army," "Heavenly Maid Scattering Flowers," "Lian Jinfeng," "Goddess of the Luo River," "The Unofficial Biography of Taizhen," "Handsome Xiren," etc. Each stage photo is accompanied by a facing page with a brief explanation in English for Western readers; (3) "The Zhuiyu Xuan," which showcases the photos of Mr. Mei's residence in Beiping, without holding back anything, such as photos of long corridors, courtyards, springs and rocks, studies, etc., all of which are extremely valuable, making the reader feel as if they are in the Zhuiyu Xuan; (4) "Mei Lanfang's Travels and Social Engagements," including photos of Mr. Mei departing for the United States and socializing with delegations in Beiping; (5) "Mei Lanfang's Calligraphy and Painting," including Mr. Mei's paintings of Buddha and recent calligraphy works. The entire book has over a hundred pages, printed with high-quality copperplate paper in two colors, with gold lettering on the cover, featuring Mr. Mei's signature. The entire book is now bound and available for special sale, priced at two yuan per copy (original price three yuan). The sales agencies (in Shanghai) are the Shishi Xinbao (Current Affairs News) on Shandong Road, the Minquan Publishing Department, and the China Travel Service on Sichuan Road. (Outside of Shanghai) Mail orders should be sent to Zhongyi Huahang, 4th Floor, Central Trust Company, No. 96 Beijing Road, Shanghai. Stamps are accepted in lieu of cash, with an additional ten cents for postage.

Peng Daxun and Others Re-sue the Fuchang Military Uniform Factory

Since the Fuchang Military Uniform Factory fire, the bereaved families, including Zhang Daxun, entrusted lawyer Yan Lunkui to file a lawsuit with the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office, requesting a legal investigation and ordering the factory to provide compensation. Many days have passed since then, but no summons have been received. Peng and others are all poor workers, and this lawsuit is a last resort. If the judicial authorities do not resolve it soon and allow them to continue suffering from the lawsuit, then their future situation would be even more unimaginable. Therefore, Lawyer Yan has drafted another petition to re-sue. The text of the petition is as follows:

To further request a strict investigation according to the law and to order compensation. This is regarding the case of Daxun and others suing Wu Desheng and others of the Fuchang Military Uniform Factory. We have repeatedly petitioned your office to resolve it quickly, but no summons have been received. Your office may consider the matter to be of great importance and should conduct a lengthy investigation. However, Daxun and others believe that the truth of the defendant's illegal acts and the tragic circumstances of the victims are already obvious and easily discernible. Moreover, the bereaved families are all poor and helpless common people, while the defendant is a capitalist with abundant savings. While a capitalist can afford a lengthy lawsuit, the poor common people are already burdened by the lawsuit. A capitalist with money may be able to escape the law, while a common person with grievances must resort to the court. Capitalists can disregard the law, while common people must rely on the law for protection. Therefore, after investigation, in terms of public prosecution, the defendant is indeed guilty of the crime in Article 187, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Code for causing the fire; in terms of closing the factory door during the fire, the defendant is indeed guilty of the provisions of Article 196 of the Criminal Code; in terms of incidental private prosecution, according to the legal provisions for calculating the age of the deceased, their income before death, and the medical and recuperation expenses of the injured, the defendant is indeed obliged to pay 48,740 yuan in compensation. Public prosecution and private prosecution, both in terms of legal principles and human sentiments, are reasons for the defendant to be blamed and there is no room for denial. Daxun and others urgently seek a resolution, like expecting clouds in a drought, and are oppressed by poverty, filled with grievances. They have a feeling that if it is not resolved in one day, there will be no relief in one day; if there is no relief in one day, there will be no survival in one day. Therefore, we do not hesitate to bother you again and present the situation. We implore your office to have a gentleman's compassion, to understand the suffering of the victims, to conduct a strict investigation according to the law quickly, and to order compensation in order to provide relief. Then the dead and the living will praise your immeasurable merits. Respectfully submitted, To the Prosecutor's Office of the Shanghai Local Court, by Peng Daxun et al., Private Prosecution Attorney Yan Lunkui, November 17th, 19th year of the Republic of China.
